// Source: 2.2 Update 4 (21UPDATE4)_CBR1.5_1735.cs
// SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers() // returns undefined
      SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers: function ()
      {
        try
        {
          var ordersToQuery = '';

          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders > option.not-processed').each(function ()
          {
            ordersToQuery += $(this).text() + ',';
          });

          /* Done creating the list of orders to get from the server which is now held in the ordersToQuery variable. */

          /* Hide the div. */
          $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').hide();

          /* Make sure there are orders in the list. */
          if (ordersToQuery.length > 0)
          {
            //ConsolidatedOrders.GetOrderInformationFromCustomer(ordersToQuery);
            Tools.MakeUserMethodRequest('GetOrderInformation', ordersToQuery, true, this.ProcessDataFromCustomer);
          }
          else
          {
            Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR: No unique orders to pull from the server.  All consolidated orders have already been added to this shipment.');
          }

        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers()', Error: error });
        }
      },

// ProcessDataFromCustomer(jsonData) // returns undefined
      ProcessDataFromCustomer: function (jsonData)
      {
        try
        {
          $(jsonData).each(function (a, b)
          {
            /* For testing, this is set to '!== true' so it will return order data.  This needs to be set to '=== true' for any other case. */
            if (ConsolidatedOrders.CheckForMatchingConsignee(b) == true)
            {
              var currentPackage = Tools.GetCurrentPackage();
              if (!currentPackage)
              {
                Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR:  Could not add commodities to package for order ' + b.orderNumber + '.  See error console for details.');
                return false;
              }
              ConsolidatedOrders.UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(b.orderNumber);
            }
            else
            {
              Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR 500:  Could not add commodities for order ' + b.orderNumber + '.  Address mismatch.');
            }
          });
        }
        catch (error)
        { 
          console.log(error);
        }
      },

// CheckForMatchingConsignee(CustomerOrderObject) // returns boolean or undefined on error
      CheckForMatchingConsignee: function (CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');

          let a = {
            //conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ',''),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          let b = {
            //conCompany: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ', ''),
            conAddress1: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: CustomerOrderObject.shipCity.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: CustomerOrderObject.shipState.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: CustomerOrderObject.shipZipCode.trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          /* Remove all the spaces in the strings so we get a good comparison, not one that's thrown off by an extra space. */
          let aa = JSON.stringify(a).replaceAll(' ', '');
          let bb = JSON.stringify(b).replaceAll(' ', '');

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          if (aa != bb)
          {
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Primary order data to follow.', Data: a });
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Subsequent order data to follow.', Data: b });
          }

          return (aa == bb);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Error: error });
        }
      },

// UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(OrderNumber) // returns undefined
      UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers: function (OrderNumber)
      {
        var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
        var inputMiscReference07 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]');
        var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val() + ',' + OrderNumber;

        var newUniqueString = Tools.GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(shipperReferenceVal);

        /* Set these input values.  ShipperReference is used by the customer, MiscReference7 is used by the SBR to update each record post-ship. */
        /* ShipperReference ONLY keeps the first order number when it goes to PostShip, before the comma, MiscReference7 keeps the entire string. */
        /* On the server-side, if MiscReference7 contains a comma, each item in the csv list gets posted back.  If MiscReference7 is empty, the ShipperReference is used instead for a single post-back. */
        $(inputShipperReference).val(newUniqueString);
        $(inputMiscReference07).val(newUniqueString);
      },

    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest){
        //retreive custom user data for Shipper Reference based on CustomData key 
        var customValue = this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User", shipmentRequest);  //this.GetShipment(shipmentRequest).UserRef1;
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = customValue;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = customValue;
    };

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        
        //create value for Shipper Reference (Ex: CustomData Reference1Value)
        var ref1Value = this.CheckReference(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1);
        //var customValue = this.CheckReference(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20);
        var customValue = this.CheckReference(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference);
        var referenceValue = customValue + " " + ref1Value;
        
        
        //set the above value for each package in the shipment
        for(var i = 0;i<shipmentRequest.Packages.length;i++){
           shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = referenceValue;
        }
        
        //check the user custom data against the validation list; if the value is not in the list, don't ship and produce an error
        this.CheckValidation(customValue, this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference20.FieldOptionValidations);
    };

// CheckReference(referenceValue) // returns string
this.CheckReference = function(referenceValue){
        if(!referenceValue)
            referenceValue = "";
        return referenceValue;
    };

// CheckValidation(referenceValue, referenceList) // returns undefined; throws an error if validation fails
this.CheckValidation = function(referenceValue, referenceList) {
        var readyToShip = false;
        for (var item in referenceList) {
            //alert(referenceList[item]);
            if (referenceList[item].Value == referenceValue) {
                readyToShip = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (readyToShip === false) throw { message: "Unable to validate shipment", errorCode: "001" };
    };

// GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) // returns string
this.GetCustom = function(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        }
        if (customDataType === "To") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
        }

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function(customField) {
                if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;

    };

// vm.shippingProfileChange(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
        vm.shippingProfileChange = function (shipmentRequest)
            {
            var tmpShippingProfile = vm.shippingProfiles.find(({ ShippingProfileName }) => ShippingProfileName === this.currentShippingProfile);
            var newShippingProfile = structuredClone(tmpShippingProfile);    
            if( newShippingProfile !== null && newShippingProfile !== undefined) {
                var selsvc = newShippingProfile.SelService;
                var myservice = {Symbol: selsvc };
                if( newShippingProfile.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery === true) {
                    newShippingProfile.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions = [4096,2048,32];                    
                }

                var today = new Date();
                var curdate = {Year: today.getFullYear(), Month: today.getMonth() + 1, Day: today.getDate()};
                newShippingProfile.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = curdate;
                this.currentShipment = newShippingProfile;
                this.selectedServices[0] = myservice;
                }
            }

// vm.CreateReturnLabelFromPrevious() // returns undefined
        vm.CreateReturnLabelFromPrevious = function ()
            {
            vm.currentShipment = structuredClone(vm.lastShipmentRequest);
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery = true;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DirectDelivery = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Proof = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ProofRequireSignature = false; 
            vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.2DA" };
            if (!vm.selectedServices) {
                vm.selectedServices = [];
            }
            vm.selectedServices.push(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service);
            };

// function validateClientMatter() // returns void
function() {

        if( theVM.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference === null) {
            alert('Client Matter field is required. Please enter a valid client matter number!');
            setFocus('input[name="ShipperReference_txt"]');            
            return;
        }
        
        var cmFound = false;
        var cm = theVM.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        var cmValidationList = theVM.fieldOptions.ShipperReference.FieldOptionValidations;
        for(var i = 0; i < cmValidationList.length; i++) {
            var cmValidationItem = cmValidationList[i];
            if( cmValidationItem.Value == cm) {
                cmFound = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if( cmFound )
            theVM.saveLicensePlate();
        else {
            alert("Client Matter field is invalid. Please enter a valid client matter number!");
            setFocus('input[name="ShipperReference_txt"]');                        
        }
    }

// function changeStateProvince(selectedCountry) // returns void
function(selectedCountry) {
                var stateProvince = client.shipping.consignee.stateProvince;
                if (stateProvince == undefined) {
                    client.alert.Danger('Custom State/Province solution does not work with FieldOption validation')
                } else {
                    var $stateProvince = $(client.shipping.consignee.stateProvinceSelector);
                    var country = $stateProvince.attr('country');
    
                    if (selectedCountry == 'US') {
                        stateProvince.$unitedStates.val('');
                        if (country == 'CA') {
                            stateProvince.$canada.replaceWith(stateProvince.$unitedStates);
                        } else if (country == 'other') {
                            stateProvince.$other.replaceWith(stateProvince.$unitedStates);
                        }
                    } else if (selectedCountry == 'CA') {
                        stateProvince.$canada.val('');
                        if (country == 'US') {
                            stateProvince.$unitedStates.replaceWith(stateProvince.$canada)
                        } else if (country == undefined || country == 'other') {
                            stateProvince.$other.replaceWith(stateProvince.$canada)
                        }  
                    } else {
                        stateProvince.$other.val('');
                        if (country == 'US') {
                            stateProvince.$unitedStates.replaceWith(stateProvince.$other);
                        } else if (country == 'CA') {
                            stateProvince.$canada.replaceWith(stateProvince.$other);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

// function updateStateProvince(country) // returns void
function(country){
                    if (this.stateProvince == undefined) {
                        var interval = setInterval(function(consignee, country) {
                            var $other = $(consignee.stateProvinceSelector)
                            if ($other.length) {
                                clearInterval(interval)
                                if ($other.attr('name') == 'StateProvince') {
                                    client.alert.Danger('Custom State/Province solution does not work with FieldOption validation')
                                } else {
                                    var attributes = {
                                        class: $other.attr('class'), 
                                        name: $other.attr('name'),
                                        type: $other.attr('type'), 
                                        required: $other.attr('required') != undefined,
                                        readonly: $other.attr('readonly') != undefined
                                    };
                                    consignee.stateProvince = {
                                        $other: $other.attr('country', 'other'),
                                        $canada: createOption('CA', attributes, client.shipping.stateProvince.canada),
                                        $unitedStates: createOption('US', attributes, client.shipping.stateProvince.unitedStates)
                                    }
                                    
                                    client.shipping.changeStateProvince(country)
                                }
                            }
                        },10, this, country)
                    }
                    $(client.shipping.consignee.stateProvinceSelector).prop('selectedIndex', 0);
                    
                    function createOption(country, attributes, list) {
                        attributes.country = country;
                        var stateProvince = $('<select />').attr(attributes);
                        stateProvince.append(new Option('','')); //add blank option
                        $.each(list, function(val, text) {
                            stateProvince.append(new Option(text, val));
                        });
                        return stateProvince;
                    }
                }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

	    // Verify all items have been packed
	    var omscheck = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;

    	// If OMS check for items not fully packed and prompt, otherwise disallow partial packs
    	if( omscheck == "OMS") {
    		if( orderItemList !== null)	{
    			var orderItemListCount1 = orderItemList.length;
    			for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount1; i++) {
    				if( orderItemList[i].qtyordered != orderItemList[i].qtyshipped ) {
    					var msg = 'SKU: ' + orderItemList[i].itemsku + ' has not been fully packed. Click OK to continue or Cancel to continue packing.';
    					var r = confirm(msg);
    					if( r === false )
    						throw Error("Ship cancelled - please continue packing.");
    				}
    			}
    		}
    	} else {
    		if( orderItemList !== null)	{
    			var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
    			for (var j = 0; j < orderItemListCount; j++) {
    				if( orderItemList[j].qtyordered != orderItemList[j].qtyshipped ) {
    					var msg2 = 'SKU: ' + orderItemList[j].itemsku + ' has not been fully packed.';
    					throw Error(msg2);
    				}
    			}
    		}
    	}
	    var itempackedlist = JSON.stringify(orderItemList);

	    //alert("itempackedlist JSONized: " + itempackedlist);

  
  	    userParams.PACKEDDATA = itempackedlist;
        };

// this.handleItemSkuTextChanged(event) // returns void
    this.handleItemSkuTextChanged = function(event) {

        var newitemsku = this.Packages[0].MiscReference10;
		if( newitemsku.trim().length === 0 )
			return;

        //debugger;
        
		//alert("Item number: " + orderItemList[1].itemcode + "  qtyordered: " + orderItemList[1].qtyordered + " qtyshipped: " + orderItemList[1].qtyshipped);

		// Check for item code SHIPCOMPLETE indicating that this order is complete
		if( newitemsku == "SHIPCOMPLETE") {

            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = "SHIPCOMPLETE";
		    //var pkg = sox_current_shipment.packages[sox_current_package_idx];
			//pkg.misc_reference_5 = "SHIPCOMPLETE";
			//$("#item_sku_txt").val("");			
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
			vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// Check for SHIP indicating that this box is complete but not the whole order
		if( newitemsku == "SHIP") {
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = "";		    
		    //var pkg = sox_current_shipment.packages[sox_current_package_idx];
			//pkg.misc_reference_5 = "";
			//$("#item_sku_txt").val("");			
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";			
			vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// Pad the input sku to 14 digits with leading zeros
		var skulen = newitemsku.length;
		var newitemskupad = "";
		if( skulen == 6)
			newitemskupad = '00000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 7)
			newitemskupad = '0000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 8)
			newitemskupad = '000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 9)
			newitemskupad = '00000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 10)
			newitemskupad = '0000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 11)
			newitemskupad = '000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 12)
			newitemskupad = '00' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 13)
			newitemskupad = '0' + newitemsku;
		else
			newitemskupad = newitemsku;
			
		newitemsku = newitemskupad;

		//alert("newitemsku: " + newitemsku);

        //alert("orderItemList length: " + orderItemList.length);
        
        //alert("orderItemList itemsku: " + orderItemList[0].itemsku);
       
       //debugger;
       
		// Verify item sku is on this order
		var itemFound = false;
		var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
		for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount; i++) {
		    if( itemFound === true)
		        break;
			var skuarr = orderItemList[i].itemsku.split(",");
			for(var j = 0; j < skuarr.length; j++) {
				if( skuarr[j] == newitemsku ) {
					itemFound = true;
					break;
				}
			}
		}
		
		//alert("itemFound: " + itemFound);
		
		if( itemFound === false) {
			ShowAlert("Pack Error","This SKU (" + newitemsku + ") does not belong in this shipment. Please remove it before proceeding.");
            $("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        			
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
            return;			
		}

		// Search for itemcode
		itemFound = false;
		var fullyPacked = false;
		var svSkuCode = "";
		var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
		for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount; i++) {
			if( itemFound == true)
				break;
			
			var nextitem = false;
			var skuarr = orderItemList[i].itemsku.split(",");
			for(var j = 0; j < skuarr.length; j++) {
				if( skuarr[j] == newitemsku ) {
					if( orderItemList[i].qtyshipped == orderItemList[i].qtyordered ) {
						fullyPacked = true;
						nextitem = true;
						break;
					} else {
						itemFound = true;
						fullyPacked = false;
						var tmpqtyshipped = Number(orderItemList[i].qtyshipped);
						var tmptotqtyshipped = Number(orderItemList[i].totqtyshipped);
						var tmpqtyordered = Number(orderItemList[i].qtyordered);
						if( (tmpqtyshipped + tmptotqtyshipped) < tmpqtyordered) {
							var calcqty1 = tmpqtyshipped + 1 + tmptotqtyshipped;
							var calcqty2 = tmpqtyordered - tmpqtyshipped - tmptotqtyshipped;
							/*alert("Calc quantity 1: " + calcqty1 + " qtyordered: " + tmpqtyordered);*/
							/*alert("Calc quantity 2: " + calcqty2);*/
							if( calcqty1 <= tmpqtyordered) {
								var tmpnewqty = tmpqtyshipped + 1;
								orderItemList[i].qtyshipped = tmpnewqty;
								orderItemList[i].modified = true;
								svSkuCode = newitemsku;
								/*alert("Item added to box ok");*/
							} else {
							    ShowAlert("Pack Error","Scanned quantity for SKU (" + newitemsku + ") would exceed order quantity. Please remove extras from the shipment and try again.");
								$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        				
                                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
                                angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
								return;						
							}
						} else {
							ShowAlert("Pack Alert","This item has been fully packed");
							$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        				
                            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
                            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
							return;						
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if( nextitem == true)
				continue;
		}

		if( fullyPacked == true) {
			ShowAlert("Pack Alert","This item has been fully packed");
			$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        			
			vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
			angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
			return;					
		}

		$("#mr10").css("background-color","Green");        	    

		//if( itemFound == false) {
		//	ShowAlert("Pack Error 2","This SKU (" + newitemsku + ") does not belong in this shipment. Please remove it before proceeding.");
		//} else {
        //    $("#mr10").css("background-color","Green");        	    
		//}

        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
        angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
		}

// Source: AMERICAN INTERNATIONAL GROUP (AIG)_Shipper Ref = Custom1_25.cs
// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
         //retreive custom user data for Shipper Reference based on CustomData key 
        var customValue;
        var CustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        
        for(var Custom in CustomData){
            if(CustomData[Custom].Key=="Custom1")customValue = CustomData[Custom].Value;
        }
       
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = customValue;
       
    }

// Source: Asia Waterjet FZCO (ASIAWATERJETFZCO)_Asia_WaterJet_CBR_1870.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        var freightfound = 0;
        var frieghterr = 0;

        for (var i = 0; i <= shipmentRequest.Packages.length - 1; i++) {
            if (parseInt(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount) >= 70) {
                freightfound = "1";
            }
            if (freightfound == "1") {
                if (parseInt(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount) < 70) {
                    frieghterr = "1";
                }
            }
        }
        if (freightfound == "0") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = {
                Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPSVR"
            }
        } else {
            if (frieghterr == "0") {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = {
                    Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPFRT"
                }
            } else {
                alert("Cannot create one shipment with 2 different service levels.");
            }
        }
        for (var i = 0; i <= shipmentRequest.Packages.length - 1; i++) {
            if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol == "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPFRT") {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Packaging = "CUSTOMER_PALLET";
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ImportDelivery = true;

        }
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country == "US") {
            if ($('select[name="CarrierInstructions"]').val() == '?') {
                alert("Please confirm shipment value");
                throw ("Excpetion");
            } else {
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference == "") {
                    if ($('select[name="CarrierInstructions"]').val() == 'string:Yes') {
                        alert("Please Enter ITN/ EES number in ConsigneeReference");
                        throw ("Excpetion");
                    }
                }
            }
        } else {
            if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country != "undefined") {
                alert("For EU Exports : Shipments above 1000 EUR, a formal export declaration is required. A formal electronic export declaration must be sent to customs authorities by the exporter or their representative. Customs authorities grant the release for export and issue an Export Accompanying Document (EAD) with a unique Movement Reference Number (MRN). The EAD has to accompany the shipment. UPS is responsible for the exit clearance at the EU border.")
            }
        }
    }

// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void; validates misc references and sets shipper reference
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams){
        // Chris Smith - Changed from Ref4 through Ref8 TO Ref2 through Ref6
        CheckValidation(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2,
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference2.FieldOptionValidations);
        CheckValidation(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3,
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference3.FieldOptionValidations);
        CheckValidation(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4,
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference4.FieldOptionValidations);
        CheckValidation(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5,
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference5.FieldOptionValidations);
        CheckValidation(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6,
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference6.FieldOptionValidations);
            
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = userID
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 + "-" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "-" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 + "-" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 + "-" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6
    }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {   
        var cont = this.ValidateShipment(shipmentRequest);
        if(!cont){
            throw {errorCode:999,message:"You cannot ship  greater than 50lb."};
        }
    }

// this.ValidateShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns boolean
this.ValidateShipment = function(shipmentRequest){
    var weight = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight;
    var weightLimit = 0;
    var totalWeight = 0;
            weightLimit = 50;
    var i;
    for(i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++)
    {
        var pkgWeight = parseFloat(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount);
        if(pkgWeight > weightLimit){
           return confirm("One or more packages is 50lb or greater.  Are you sure you want to continue?");
        //throw {errorCode:999,message:"You cannot ship  greater than " + weightLimit + " " + weight.Units + "."};
    } else{
        return true;
    }
    }

}

// this.ValidatePackage(pkg) // returns void
this.ValidatePackage = function(pkg){
    debugger;
    var weight = pkg.Weight;
    var weightLimit = 0;
    var totalWeight = 0;
            weightLimit = 50;

        var pkgWeight = parseFloat(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        if(pkgWeight > weightLimit){
            alert("Previous package weight is greater than 50lb.");
        } 
    }

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
        debugger;
      this.ValidatePackage(shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1]);
    }

// Source: Boston Scientific (BOSTON)_Admin_Profile_CBR_2481.cs
// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {  
     // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
     // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
      debugger;
      
       //cm=in/0.39370
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         
         if(pkg.Dimensions === undefined || pkg.Dimensions.Units === undefined ||  pkg.Dimensions.Length === undefined ||  pkg.Dimensions.Width === undefined ||  pkg.Dimensions.Height === undefined){
           throw Error('ERROR:' + " Missing Dimensions");
         }
         
         
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
         }
         
     });
      
      
     //kg = lbs*0.453592    
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
     });
     
      if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
   
    }

// Source: Boston Scientific (BOSTON)_Boston Coyol Client Business Rules_2474.cs
// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
  
    // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
    // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
    debugger;
    //kg = lbs*0.453592 
    totalShipWeight = 0;
    totalVolumetricResult = 0;
    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
    });
              
    totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
    console.log(totalShipWeight);
    console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
    if (totalShipWeight > 150)
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Shipment Weight Limit of 150lbs")
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule " + totalShipWeight);
    }
    
    if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Limit of " + Number(maxvolumetric))
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Rule " + Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2));
    }
    
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
     });
     
    //cm=in/0.39370
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
         }
         
     });
     
     
    // debugger;
      if(Number(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount).toFixed(2) > 2500 ){
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = "OS";
          }
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
              $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
              throw new Error('Missing AES/ITN Number');
          } 
          if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
      }
     
    console.log(shipmentRequest);
  
};

// function ShippingLoaded() // returns void
this.ShippingLoaded = function(){
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress;
    this.vm.serviceOption = serviceOption;
    this.vm.serviceOptions = serviceOptions(this.vm.profile);
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
   

    function serviceOption() {
        this.selectedServices = [this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service];
    }
    function serviceOptions(profile) {
        //debugger;
        var filterServices = [];
        var customData3 = uPS_Service.split(',');
        for (var item of customData3) {
            var symbol = getServiceSymbol(item.toLowerCase());
            for (var service of profile.Services) {
                if (service.Symbol === symbol) {
                    service.Name = service.Name.replace('(UPS Adapter)','').trim();
                    if (service.Name.includes("Expedited")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (MAIN SERVICE)";
                    }
                    if (service.Name.includes("Saver")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (Only with Boston's Authorization)";
                    }
                    filterServices.push(service);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return filterServices;
        function getServiceSymbol(code) {
            if (code == '2dn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.2DA'
            else if (code == '3dd') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.3DS'
            else if (code == 'exp') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'ess') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'nda') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDA'
            else if (code == 'dae') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDAEAM'
            else if (code == 'grn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.GND'
            else if (code == 'uwe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'wep') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESSSP'
            else if (code == 'swe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'uws') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER'
            else if (code == 'std') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD'
        }
        
    }
    
    if(dims.includes(',')){
        var dimensions = dims.split(',');
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount = Number(dimensions[0]);
        maxvolumetric = Number(dimensions[4]);
        console.log("Max Volumetric: " + maxvolumetric);
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Dimensions = {
            Length: Number(dimensions[1]),
            Height: Number(dimensions[2]),
            Width: Number(dimensions[3]),
            Units: 0
        };
    }
   
    vm = this.vm;
};

// function GetShipFromAddresses() // returns AddressBookEntries array
this.GetShipFromAddresses = function(){
    var payloadShipFromAddress = {
        "Skip": 0,
        "Take": 0,
        "WhereClauses": [{
           "FieldName": "Code",
                    "FieldValue": sf_AddressType,   //'ze-'
                    "Operator": 6
                }]
    };
 
    var sfdata = {
        CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
        addressBookIds: shipFromAddressBookId,
        SearchCriteria: payloadShipFromAddress
    };
   
    ShipFromAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', sfdata, false).responseJSON;
    
     //debugger;
    
    for(let i = 0; i < ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
    
        ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Code = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Code.replace("&amp;",'&');
        ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company.replace("&amp;",'&');
   }


    console.log(ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries);
    
    return ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries;
};

        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].SedMethod = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SedMethod;
}

// function RemovePackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.RemovePackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
      var totalShipWeight = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
      });
      totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
      document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
      
      var totalVolumetricResult = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
           totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
      });
      totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
      $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
      document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
      if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
        {
           $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
           throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
        }
  
}

    };
    //console.log(data);
  
    ShipToAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', data, false).responseJSON;

    console.log(ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries);
    
    return ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries;
            
};

// function GetShipFromAddresses() // returns address book entries array
this.GetShipFromAddresses = function(){
    var payloadShipFromAddress = {
        "Skip": 0,
        "Take": 0,
        "WhereClauses": [{
           "FieldName": "Code",
                    "FieldValue": sf_AddressType,   //'ze-'
                    "Operator": 6
                }]
    };
 
    var sfdata = {
        CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
        addressBookIds: shipFromAddressBookId,
        SearchCriteria: payloadShipFromAddress
    };
   
    ShipFromAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', sfdata, false).responseJSON;
    
     //debugger;
    
    for(let i = 0; i < ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
    
        ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Code = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Code.replace("&amp;",'&');
        ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company.replace("&amp;",'&');
   }


    console.log(ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries);
    
    return ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries;
};

this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {

// function RemovePackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
this.RemovePackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
      
      var totalShipWeight = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
      });
      totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
      document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
      
      var totalVolumetricResult = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
           totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
      });
      totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
      $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
      document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
      if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
        {
           $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
           throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
        }
  
      
}

// Source: Boston Scientific (BOSTON)_Boston_MULTI_2485.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined; validates shipment weight/dimensions and converts lb/in to kg/cm
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
  
    // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
     // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
     // debugger;
     
     totalShipWeight = 0;
    totalVolumetricResult = 0;
    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
    });
              
    totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
    console.log(totalShipWeight);
    console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
    if (totalShipWeight > 150)
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Shipment Weight Limit of 150lbs")
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule " + totalShipWeight);
    }
    
    if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Limit of " + Number(maxvolumetric))
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Rule " + Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2));
    }
     
     //kg = lbs*0.453592    
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
     });
     
    //cm=in/0.39370
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
         }
         
     });
     
     
    // debugger;
      if(Number(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount).toFixed(2) > 2500 ){
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = "OS";
          }
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
              $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
              throw new Error('Missing AES/ITN Number');
          } 
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Comments = vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
      }
     
    console.log(shipmentRequest);
  
};

// function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// Source: Cabinet Works Group (MASCO)_Masco Client Side Business Rules_1752.cs
// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    // 🔄 Reset any previous SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = "";

    // 🧾 First prompt: general input
    var firstInput = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###)\n' +
        '— OR type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip dimensions\n' +
        '— OR enter a SWOG Order Number to start the SWOG function:',
        ''
    );

    if (firstInput === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";
        return;  // ❌ Cancelled
    }

    firstInput = firstInput.trim();
    var dimRegex = /^[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+$/i;

    if (firstInput.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';
        return;  // ✅ Skip dimensions
    }

    if (dimRegex.test(firstInput)) {
        userParams.dimensions = firstInput.toLowerCase();
        return;  // ✅ Valid dimensions directly
    }

    // 🌀 Else: treat as SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = firstInput;
    this.vm.swogShipment();

    // 🧾 Second prompt after SWOG
    var dimsAfterSwog = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###), type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip, or leave blank:',
        ''
    );

    if (dimsAfterSwog === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Cancelled
        return;
    }

    dimsAfterSwog = dimsAfterSwog.trim();

    if (dimsAfterSwog.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';  // ✅ PACKSIZE_CONTINUE accepted in second prompt too
    } else if (dimRegex.test(dimsAfterSwog)) {
        userParams.dimensions = dimsAfterSwog.toLowerCase();  // ✅ Dimensions entered
    } else {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Nothing valid entered
    }
}

// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        thinClient.loading.show();
        thinClient.dismiss.All();
        userParams.customer = this.vm.shipping.customer.value;
        userParams.labelImage = this.vm.labelImage;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference15 = thinClient.today();
    }

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        thinClient.loading.hide();
        this.vm.labelImage = null;


        if (this.vm.shipping.customer.value == 'AMAZON') {
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ConsigneeReference.IsDisabled = true;
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ShipperReference.IsDisabled = true;
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsDisabled = true;

            if (this.vm.loadValue == 'Return') {
                this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsDisabled = false;
                //this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = true;
            }
        }

        if((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage ?? '').includes('Invalid Service Option')) {
            this.vm.shipping.activePanel = 0;
            this.vm.shipping.panelMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
        }
        this.vm.loadValue = null;
    }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {   
        debugger;
        var usCountry = "UNITED_STATES";
        var usAcronym = "US";
        var PackageRequests=shipmentRequest.Packages;
        
        $(PackageRequests).each(function (x, item)
          {
              var value = item.DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount;
              var tN = item.AesTransactionNumber;
              if (value >= 2500 && tN ===null)
              {
                    alert("Please check with clarios-na-trade@clarios.com if EEI filing is needed");
              }             
             item.Description=$('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val();
            
          });
          
          // For International Destination Rule Applies to all use cases and all carriers
          if ((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usCountry) && (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usAcronym))
                {
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "Y";
                }
                else
                {
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "N";
                }
             
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (cbr.historyShipment != null) {
            var historyRequest = JSON.parse(cbr.historyShipment);
            this.vm.totalPackages = historyRequest.Packages.length;

            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults = historyRequest.PackageDefaults;
            shipmentRequest.Packages = historyRequest.Packages;
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Description = "PC Equipment";

            shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg) {
                pkg.ReturnDelivery = true;
                pkg.ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
                pkg.ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = historyRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
                pkg.Description = "PC Equipment";
            });
            cbr.historyShipment = null;
        }
        cbr.bulk.create.itemReferences = [];
    }

				let width = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width;
				let height = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height;
				let units = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units === 0 ? "IN" : "CM";
				$('#newDimensions').val(length + "x" + width + "x" + height + " " + units);
				
				if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					$('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"').prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
			else {
				$('#newDimensions').val('');
			}
		});
		$('#newDimensions').val('');
		$('#newDimensions').keyup(function(e) {
			let loadButton = $('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"');
			if (this.value.trim() === '' && vmTemp.loadValue) {
				loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
			}
			else {
				// enforce dimensions mask if entered LxWxH (IN/CM optional)
				let regEx = /(\d+)x(\d+)x(\d+)( IN| CM)?/
				if (!regEx.test(this.value)) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', true);
				}
				else if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
		});

		// show Load Shipment dialog and set focus
		if (!$('#newShipmentDialog').is(':visible')) {
			$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('show');
			$('#newShipmentDialog').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
				$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
			});
		}
	};

// function PreLoad(value, shipmentRequest, params) // returns undefined
this.PreLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest, params) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === null) {
			// if box is empty, add custom dimensions from dialog
			let dims = $('#newDimensions').val().trim().split(/x| /);
			if (dims !== null && dims.length >= 3) {
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="length"]').val(dims[0]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="width"]').val(dims[1]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="height"]').val(dims[2]).change();
				
				let index = 1;
				if (dims.length === 4) {
					dims[3] = dims[3].toUpperCase();
					index = (dims[3] === 'IN' ? 1 : 2);
				}
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('select[name="units"] option:eq(' + index + ')').prop('selected', true);
			}
		}

		let oChk = this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20;		// autoship
		if (oChk === true) {
			params.autoship = oChk;
		}

		$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('hide');
		showLoading(true);
	};

// function PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		debugger;
		let errorMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
		
		if (errorMessage === undefined) errorMessage = "";
		if (errorMessage === null) errorMessage = "";

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === "x") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("No service selected!");
		}
		
		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage === 'validate') {
			//$("#ctl00_cphContent_left_tabs_consignee_tab_consignee_na_ab_ctrl_na_ctrl_validate_addr_btn").click();
			showLoading(false);
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage.substring(0, 4) === "pop:") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage !== '') {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage);
			let errors = ["not found", "already shipped", "too many"];
			if (errors.some(errorText => errorMessage.includes(errorText))) {
				// open Load Shipment dialog
				this.vm.newShipment();
			}
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}

		$("#custom_markup_id").val(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);

		//getWeight();

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship') {
			this.vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// select all services before rate
		setTimeout(function() {
			// check Select All after delay to allow UI update
			vmTemp.isAllServicesSelected = true;
			vmTemp.selectAllServices();
			vmTemp.rate();
		}, 100);
		
	};

// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
		console.log("🚀 [PreShip] Starting PreShip function...");
	    shipmentRequest = vmTemp.currentShipment;
		// Validate shipmentRequest and Packages array
		if (!shipmentRequest || !shipmentRequest.Packages || !Array.isArray(shipmentRequest.Packages)) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			//alert("[PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			return;
		}
	
		let validDimensions = [];
	
		console.log(`📦 [PreShip] Processing ${shipmentRequest.Packages.length} package(s)...`);
	
		// Retrieve current package dimensions from vmTemp
		try {
			let currentPackage = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex];
			if (!currentPackage || !currentPackage.Dimensions) {
				console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] vmTemp.currentShipment package or dimensions not found.");
			} else {
				let dims = currentPackage.Dimensions;
				console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Current Package Dimensions from vmTemp: ${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`);
			}
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Unable to retrieve package dimensions from vmTemp.");
		}
	
		// Loop through all packages to validate their dimensions
		for (let i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
			console.log(`🔍 [PreShip] Checking package at index ${i}...`);
	
			let packageData = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
	
			if (!packageData) {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				return;
			}
	
			if (!packageData.Dimensions) {
				console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				return;
			}
	
			let dims = packageData.Dimensions;
	
			// Ensure all dimension values exist and are valid numbers
			if (dims.Length > 0 && dims.Width > 0 && dims.Height > 0) {
				let dimensionString = `${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`; // Always append "0"
	
				// Validate format (three numeric values + "0" at the end)
				let dimParts = dimensionString.split(new RegExp("[x ]"), 4); // Split on 'x' and space
	
				if (dimParts.length === 4 && !isNaN(dimParts[0]) && !isNaN(dimParts[1]) && !isNaN(dimParts[2]) && dimParts[3] === "0") {
					validDimensions.push(dimensionString);
					console.log(`✅ [PreShip] Package ${i} Dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
				} else {
					console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
					//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions.`);
					return;
				}
			} else {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				return;
			}
		}
	
		// Store only valid dimensions in MiscReference5
		if (validDimensions.length > 0) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = validDimensions.join(", ");
			console.log(`✅ [PreShip] All dimensions successfully stored in MiscReference5: ${shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5}`);
		} else {
			console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] No packages had valid dimensions.");
		}
	
		// Retrieve weight and markup values
		userParams.weight = $('div[caption="Weight"]').find('input[name="unitValue_txt"]').val();
		userParams.markup = $("#custom_markup_id").val();
		console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Retrieved weight: ${userParams.weight}, Markup: ${userParams.markup}`);
	
		// Custom code to hide/filter on postship errors - must be started here
		$("<style> .alert-danger { display: none; } </style>").appendTo("head");
		console.log("🚫 [PreShip] Hidden alert-danger elements to prevent UI issues.");
	
		alertInterval = setInterval(function () {
			var errAlert = $('div.alert-danger');
		
			// Filter and show alert
			if (errAlert.length > 0) {
				clearInterval(alertInterval);
				let msg = errAlert.text();
				if (msg.indexOf('-1') === -1 && msg.indexOf('CONNECTSHIP') === -1) {
					errAlert.show();
					console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] PostShip Alert Detected: ${msg}`);
				}
			}
		}, 200);
	
		console.log("✅ [PreShip] Function completed successfully.");
	};

// this.PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        var stName;
        var vmExists = false;

        var customData1 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom1");
        var customData2 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom2");
        var customData3 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom3");

        if (typeof objVM === "undefined") {
            stName = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = customData2 + "~" + stName;
        } else {
            vmExists = true;
            stName = objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
            objVM.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = isDefined(customData2) + "~" + stName;
        }
        // alert("customData2 = " + customData2);


        if (isDefined(customData3) == "FC") {
            if (vmExists === true) {
                objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            } else {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            }
            nameaddress.Account = isDefined(customData1);
        }

        function PullCustomData(consignee, field) {
            //alert(JSON.stringify(consignee));

            for (var item in consignee) {
                if (consignee[item].Key == field) return consignee[item].Value;
            }
        }

        function isDefined(referenceValue) {
            var goodValue = null;
            if (typeof referenceValue == "undefined" ||
                referenceValue === null) {
                goodValue = "";
            } else {
                goodValue = referenceValue;
            }
            return goodValue;
        }
    };

    };

// this.PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreRate = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg) {
            // Updates code to get UserId from the vm instead of an API call
            pkg.MiscReference20 = vm.UserInformation.UserId;  
        });

        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            var sfState = getStateAbbreviation(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince);
            if (sfState !== null &&
                typeof sfState !== "undefined") {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince = sfState;
            }
        }
    };

// this.AddEmailToNotification(event) // returns void
    this.AddEmailToNotification = function (event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = getShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    }

// function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns void
        function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns void
    function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {

                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;

                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')

// function getShipmentEmailAddresses(def) // returns an emailAddress object with Consignee/Origin fields when available
    function getShipmentEmailAddresses(def) {
        var emailAddress = {}
        if (def.Consignee.Email != undefined && def.Consignee.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Consignee = def.Consignee.Email;
        }
        if (def.OriginAddress != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Origin = def.OriginAddress.Email;
        }
        return emailAddress;
    }

// function getStateAbbreviation(state) // returns a two-letter state/province abbreviation or undefined
    function getStateAbbreviation(state)
    {
        var stateFullNameList = { "arizona": "AZ", "alabama": "AL", "alaska": "AK", "arkansas": "AR", "california": "CA", "colorado": "CO", "connecticut": "CT", "districtofcolumbia": "DC", "delaware": "DE", "florida": "FL", "georgia": "GA", "hawaii": "HI", "idaho": "ID", "illinois": "IL", "indiana": "IN", "iowa": "IA", "kansas": "KS", "kentucky": "KY", "louisiana": "LA", "maine": "ME", "maryland": "MD", "massachusetts": "MA", "michigan": "MI", "minnesota": "MN", "mississippi": "MS", "missouri": "MO", "montana": "MT", "nebraska": "NE", "nevada": "NV", "newhampshire": "NH", "newjersey": "NJ", "newmexico": "NM", "newyork": "NY", "northcarolina": "NC", "northdakota": "ND", "ohio": "OH", "oklahoma": "OK", "oregon": "OR", "pennsylvania": "PA", "rhodeisland": "RI", "southcarolina": "SC", "southdakota": "SD", "tennessee": "TN", "texas": "TX", "utah": "UT", "vermont": "VT", "virginia": "VA", "washington": "WA", "westvirginia": "WV", "wisconsin": "WI", "wyoming": "WY", "alberta": "AB", "britishcolumbia": "BC", "manitoba": "MB", "newbrunswick": "NB", "newfoundland": "NF", "northwestterritory": "NT", "novascotia": "NS", "nunavut": "NU", "ontario": "ON", "princeedwardisland": "PE", "quebec": "QC", "saskatchewan": "SK", "yukon": "YT" }
        if (state == undefined) return state;
        if (state.trim().length == 2) return state;
        var stateFullName = state.toLowerCase().replace(/\ /g, '');
        return stateFullNameList[stateFullName];
    }

// function setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) // returns void
    function setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) {
        var isInternational = nameAddress.Country != 'US';
        $('[property="Packaging"] select').prop('disabled', isInternational);
        if (isInternational) {
            var packages = shipmentRequest.Packages;
            for (var i = 0; i < packages.length; i++) {
                packages[i].Packaging = 'LETTER';
            }
        }
    }

// function getStateAbbreviation(state) // returns a state abbreviation or the original state value
    function getStateAbbreviation(state)
    {
        var stateFullNameList = { "arizona": "AZ", "alabama": "AL", "alaska": "AK", "arkansas": "AR", "california": "CA", "colorado": "CO", "connecticut": "CT", "districtofcolumbia": "DC", "delaware": "DE", "florida": "FL", "georgia": "GA", "hawaii": "HI", "idaho": "ID", "illinois": "IL", "indiana": "IN", "iowa": "IA", "kansas": "KS", "kentucky": "KY", "louisiana": "LA", "maine": "ME", "maryland": "MD", "massachusetts": "MA", "michigan": "MI", "minnesota": "MN", "mississippi": "MS", "missouri": "MO", "montana": "MT", "nebraska": "NE", "nevada": "NV", "newhampshire": "NH", "newjersey": "NJ", "newmexico": "NM", "newyork": "NY", "northcarolina": "NC", "northdakota": "ND", "ohio": "OH", "oklahoma": "OK", "oregon": "OR", "pennsylvania": "PA", "rhodeisland": "RI", "southcarolina": "SC", "southdakota": "SD", "tennessee": "TN", "texas": "TX", "utah": "UT", "vermont": "VT", "virginia": "VA", "washington": "WA", "westvirginia": "WV", "wisconsin": "WI", "wyoming": "WY", "alberta": "AB", "britishcolumbia": "BC", "manitoba": "MB", "newbrunswick": "NB", "newfoundland": "NF", "northwestterritory": "NT", "novascotia": "NS", "nunavut": "NU", "ontario": "ON", "princeedwardisland": "PE", "quebec": "QC", "saskatchewan": "SK", "yukon": "YT" }
        if (state == undefined) return state;
        if (state.trim().length == 2) return state;
        var stateFullName = state.toLowerCase().replace(/\ /g, '');
        var returnStateAbbreviation = stateFullNameList[stateFullName];
        if (returnStateAbbreviation == undefined) return state;
        return returnStateAbbreviation;
    }

        }
    };

        }
    }

// this.ConsigneeCountryChange() // returns void

        setInternationalPackaging(this.currentShipment, this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee);
    }

// function setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) // returns void
    function setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) {
        var isInternational = nameAddress.Country != 'US';
        $('[property="Packaging"] select').prop('disabled', isInternational);
        if (isInternational) {
            var packages = shipmentRequest.Packages;
            for (var i = 0; i < packages.length; i++) {
                packages[i].Packaging = 'LETTER';
            }
        }
    }

// function getStateAbbreviation(state) // returns state abbreviation or original state
    function getStateAbbreviation(state)
    {
        var stateFullNameList = { "arizona": "AZ", "alabama": "AL", "alaska": "AK", "arkansas": "AR", "california": "CA", "colorado": "CO", "connecticut": "CT", "districtofcolumbia": "DC", "delaware": "DE", "florida": "FL", "georgia": "GA", "hawaii": "HI", "idaho": "ID", "illinois": "IL", "indiana": "IN", "iowa": "IA", "kansas": "KS", "kentucky": "KY", "louisiana": "LA", "maine": "ME", "maryland": "MD", "massachusetts": "MA", "michigan": "MI", "minnesota": "MN", "mississippi": "MS", "missouri": "MO", "montana": "MT", "nebraska": "NE", "nevada": "NV", "newhampshire": "NH", "newjersey": "NJ", "newmexico": "NM", "newyork": "NY", "northcarolina": "NC", "northdakota": "ND", "ohio": "OH", "oklahoma": "OK", "oregon": "OR", "pennsylvania": "PA", "rhodeisland": "RI", "southcarolina": "SC", "southdakota": "SD", "tennessee": "TN", "texas": "TX", "utah": "UT", "vermont": "VT", "virginia": "VA", "washington": "WA", "westvirginia": "WV", "wisconsin": "WI", "wyoming": "WY", "alberta": "AB", "britishcolumbia": "BC", "manitoba": "MB", "newbrunswick": "NB", "newfoundland": "NF", "northwestterritory": "NT", "novascotia": "NS", "nunavut": "NU", "ontario": "ON", "princeedwardisland": "PE", "quebec": "QC", "saskatchewan": "SK", "yukon": "YT" }
        if (state == undefined) return state;
        if (state.trim().length == 2) return state;
        var stateFullName = state.toLowerCase().replace(/\ /g, '');
        var returnStateAbbreviation = stateFullNameList[stateFullName];
        if (returnStateAbbreviation == undefined) return state;
        return returnStateAbbreviation;
    }

  this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {

    /* Don Beal (dbeal@ups.com) */

  }

// function CheckForRequiredValues() // returns boolean
    function CheckForRequiredValues()
    {
      var bValid = true;

      if ($('#inputclient').val().trim().length == 0)
      {
        $('#inputclient').addClass('has-error');
        bValid = false;
        UIMethods.SwitchToTab(0);
      }

      /* If the 3rd party billing checkbox is checked, all the text fields need to be filled out. */
      if (($('#checkboxthirdparty').prop('checked') == true) && (bValid == true))
      {
        var textBoxes = $('#tabThirdPartyBilling input[type=text]');
        $(textBoxes).each(function(x, y)
        {
          if ($(this).val().trim().length == 0)
          {
            $(this).addClass('has-error');
            bValid = false;
            UIMethods.SwitchToTab(2);
          }
        });
      }

      return bValid;
    }

// UpdateCurrentBatch() // returns void
      UpdateCurrentBatch: function()
      {
        if (CheckForRequiredValues() == false) { return false; }

        //var UserMethod = {};
        //UserMethod.ServerMethod = 'UpdateBatchData';

        var dataObject = {};

        dataObject.BatchReference = $('.batch-id').text();
        dataObject.Shipper = $('#selectshippers option:selected').val();
        dataObject.PackageType = $('#selectpackagetype option:selected').val();
        dataObject.DeliveryConfirmation = $('#checkboxdeliveryconfirmation').prop('checked');
        dataObject.SignatureRequired = $('#deliveryconfirmationcontainer input[type=radio]:checked').val();
        dataObject.BillingOption = $('#selectbilling option:selected').val();

        dataObject.Telephone = $('#inputphone').val();
        dataObject.PackageWeight = $('#inputweight').val();
        dataObject.PackageDeclaredValue = $('#inputdeclared').val();
        dataObject.Client = $('#inputclient').val();
        dataObject.GoodsDescription = $('#inputgoods').val();
        dataObject.ConsigneeAccount = $('#inputaccountnumber').val();

        dataObject.DomesticServiceMethod = $('#selectdomesticservice option:selected').val();
        dataObject.InternationalServiceMethod = $('#selectintlservice option:selected').val();
        dataObject.DomesticSaturday = $('#checkboxdomesticsaturdaydel').prop('checked');
        dataObject.DomesticInternational = $('#checkboxintlsaturdaydel').prop('checked');

        dataObject.ThirdPartyBilling = false;

        if ($('#checkboxthirdparty').prop('checked') == true)
        {
          /* Need to add 3rd party billing data. */
          dataObject.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
          dataObject.ThirdPartyCompany = $('#inputThirdPartyCompany').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyContact = $('#inputThirdPartyContact').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAddress1 = $('#inputThirdPartyAddress1').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAddress2 = $('#inputThirdPartyAddress2').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAddress3 = $('#inputThirdPartyAddress3').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyCity = $('#inputThirdPartyCity').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyState = $('#inputThirdPartyState').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyPostalCode = $('#inputThirdPartyPostalCode').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAccount = $('#inputThirdPartyAccount').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyCountry = $('#selectThirdPartyCountry option:selected').val().replace("string:", "");
        }

        this.MakeUserMethodRequest('UpdateBatchData', dataObject).then(function() { $('#divCustomTabContainer').fadeOut(); });

        //UserMethod.MethodData = dataObject;
      }
