// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    //debugger;
    loadValue = loadValue.replace('!!', '');

    if (typeof shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== 'undefined' && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5.length > 2)
    {
      alertMessage('danger', shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5);
    }

    this.vm.getWeight();
    //$("#overrideRateShopping_Y").prop("checked", true);

    // Warn user if expedited service selected and PO box is checked
    const expServices = "UPS.NDA,UPS.2AM,UPS.2DA,UPS.EXP,USPS.PRIORITY,USPS.EXPR".split(',');

    let hasExpedited = expServices.some(service => shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol.includes(service));
    if (hasExpedited && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PoBox)
    {
      alertMessage('warning', "Order " + loadValue + " has an Expedited service selected but a PO box was used. Contact Customer Service for a new address.")
    }

    // if Int'l shipment, show Assign Commodities button, hide Add Package button group, and init AssignGoods
    //sna6dxb - 09-23-2022
    //don't need this any longer, the button is hidden by default in the template
    //$('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country !== "US")
    {
      $('#btnAssignCommodities').show();
      $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().hide();
      const Goods = new AssignGoods(this.vm);
    }
    else {
        // ensure Assign Commodities button is hidden in case they load an Int'l order by mistake, then load domestic
        $('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
        $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().show();
    }
  }

// ShowAssignGoodsPane() // returns void
  ShowAssignGoodsPane()
  {
    let that = this;
    //get rid of any previous entries
    $('#listItemContainer li:gt(0)').remove();

    //change the column width to make the descriptions longer
    //change this back when the user clicks the 'Apply' button
    $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6')

    //set a reference to the packages object as well as the commodities objects
    this.packages = this.viewModel.currentShipment.Packages;

    //get all the commodities in the shipment from all packages
    this.goods = $(this.packages).map(function(x, y)
    {
      return y.CommodityContents;
    });

    //loop the goods array and update the markup within the slideout panel
    $(this.goods).each(function(a, b)
    {
      //debugger;
      let k = 'e' + (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
      b.GoodsKey = k;

      if (b.packageIndex === undefined) {
        // initial index is undefined after loading order, default to fix NaN bug later
        b.packageIndex = 0;
      }
      //copy the source element
      let item = $('#liClone').clone(true).attr({ 'hash-key': b.$$hashKey, 'goods-key': b.GoodsKey, 'pkg-index': b.packageIndex }).removeAttr('id');

      //the customer is sending amounts that have sometimes 10 digits after the decimal point which is throwing exceptions when trying
      //to parseFloat so this is the simplest way to get around that.
      let cost = Math.round(b.UnitValue.Amount * 100) / 100;

      $(item).find('.goods-description').text(b.Description);
      $(item).find('.goods-quantity').html('(<strong>' + b.Quantity + '</strong>');
      $(item).find('.goods-unit-of-measure').text(b.QuantityUnitMeasure + ', ');
      $(item).find('.goods-declared-value').html('<strong>$' + cost + '</strong> ' + b.UnitValue.Currency + ')');
      $(item).find('.pkg-index-text').text(+(b.packageIndex) + 1);
      $(item).find('.header-logo').show();

      //append it to our list
      $('#divAssignCommodities ul.list-group').append(item);

      //show it gracefully
      $(item).show();

    });

    //create a working array object so we can manipulate the data non-destructively
    this.working = $.makeArray(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(this.goods)));

    $('#divAssignCommodities').show().animate({ left: 0 }, 400);
    $('.assign-to-pkg:visible').first().focus();
  }

// UpdateGoodsObject(pkgCount, listItem) // returns void
  UpdateGoodsObject(pkgCount, listItem)
  {
    const itemkey = $(listItem).attr('hash-key');
    const goodkey = $(listItem).attr('goods-key');
    const findex = +$(listItem).attr('pkg-index');

    let val = $(listItem).find('.goods-declared-value');
    let cost = $(val).find('strong').text().replace('$', '');

    cost = (cost / pkgCount).toFixed(2);

    //get the object that matches the hash-key from the working array
    //this will be the template to use when creating new packages after a split operation
    //working on a copy of the vm commodity object so we can abandon changes if needed
    let src = $.grep(this.working, function(value, i) { return value.$$hashKey == itemkey; })[0];

    //update the declared value for the first package
    src.UnitValue.Amount = cost;

    for (let y = 1; y < pkgCount; y++)
    {
      let ccobj = this.GetNewCommodityObject(src);
      ccobj.packageIndex = findex + y;

      this.working.push(ccobj);

      this.UpdateScreenMarkup(ccobj, listItem);
    }
  }

// UpdateScreenMarkup(ccobj, li) // returns void
  UpdateScreenMarkup(ccobj, li)
  {
    //this is all setting up the first list item to be cloned in the next function
    //hide the split button
    $(li).find('.btn-show-split-form').fadeOut();

    //show the input for number of items in this pkg
    $(li).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg').fadeIn();

    //display the header
    $(li).find('.header-logo').css('display', 'block');

    $(li).find('.goods-declared-value').html('<strong>$' + ccobj.UnitValue.Amount + '</strong> ' + 'USD' + ')');

    this.CreateListViewItem(ccobj.packageIndex, li)

    let input = $('#listItemContainer').find('.num-of-items-in-pkg');
    $(input).tooltip({ container: 'body' });

    //when done creating elements, focus on the first visible non-disabled input box
    $('#listItemContainer').find($('.num-of-items-in-pkg:visible:not(:disabled)').first().focus());

    //if there was a single item (i.e a KIT), split evenly and close
    let qty = +$(li).find('.goods-quantity strong').text();
    if (qty === 1)
    {
      let these = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[goods-key=' + $(li).attr('goods-key') + ']');
      $(these).attr('pkg-status', 'packed');
      $(these).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg').val(1).attr('disabled', 'disabled');
      $(these).find('.goods-quantity > strong').text(1);
      $(these).find('.split-pkgs-modal').hide().find('input').val([]);
      //$('#btnApplyCommodityAssignments').trigger('click');
    }
  }

// CreateListViewItem(idx, li) // returns void
  CreateListViewItem(idx, li)
  {
    //the hash-key attr is the object id for the commodity in relation to the package
    //if we keep it, all packages will have the same hash-key (pkg 0)
    let item = $(li).clone(true).removeAttr('hash-key').removeAttr('id');
    $(item).attr('pkg-index', idx);

    $(item).find('.pkg-index-text').text(idx + 1);
    $(item).find('.goods-quantity').html('(<strong>0</strong>');

    let lastInList = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[goods-key="' + $(li).attr('goods-key') + '"]').last();

    //i have no idea why the opacity changes when i use .show().  first time i've ever seen that.
    //anyway, set it implicitly here so the element shows
    $(item).appendTo('#listItemContainer').insertAfter(lastInList).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg').css('opacity', '1').show();
  }

// UpdatePkgCountsInWorkingObject(li) // returns void
  UpdatePkgCountsInWorkingObject(li)
  {
    let goodkey = $(li).attr('goods-key');
    let pkgindex = $(li).attr('pkg-index');
    let itemcount = $(li).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg').val();

    //find the object in this.working that has the matching pkg-index and goods-key, then update it
    let w = $.grep(this.working, function(pkg, i) { return pkg.GoodsKey == goodkey && pkg.packageIndex == pkgindex  })[0];

    w.Quantity = itemcount;
  }

// UpdateListItemPackageQuantities(li) // returns void
  UpdateListItemPackageQuantities(li)
  {
    this.UpdatePkgCountsInWorkingObject(li);

    let numOfItems = $(li).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg');
    let remItems = $(li).find('.goods-quantity > strong');

    if (!$(numOfItems).val()) { return; }

    let x = (+$(remItems).text() - $(numOfItems).val());

    //sanity check to make sure we didn't pack more items that we had
    if (x < 0)
    {
      $(remItems).addClass('bad-math');
      return;
    }

    $(remItems).removeClass('bad-math');
    $(numOfItems).attr('disabled', 'disabled');
    $(li).attr('pkg-status', 'packed');

    //move to the next list item and update then focus
    $(li).next().find('.goods-quantity > strong').text(x)

    //on the second-to-last list item, use the input value to auto-set the last item
    //to get the number of rows that have already been assigned, count the list items with the goods-key
    //that have disabled input boxes
    let rowsForThisGood = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[goods-key="' + $(li).attr('goods-key') + '"]');
    let rowsDone = $(rowsForThisGood).find('input:disabled:visible').length;

    if (rowsForThisGood.length == (rowsDone + 1))
    {
      let lastLi = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[goods-key="' + $(li).attr('goods-key') + '"]').last();

      $(lastLi).attr('pkg-status', 'packed');

      let lastVal = $(li).next().find('.goods-quantity > strong').text();
      $(lastLi).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg').val(lastVal).attr('disabled', 'disabled');

      $('#listItemContainer').find('.assign-to-pkg:visible').first().focus();

      this.UpdatePkgCountsInWorkingObject(lastLi);
    }
  }

// ApplyCommodityAssignments() // returns void
  ApplyCommodityAssignments()
  {
    let that = this;

    //every list item will have a pkg-index attr, get that highest value to determine how many pkgs we need
    //don't use pkg-status.length because that will include multiple commodities and the end result will be wrong
    let packed = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[pkg-status=packed]');

    //first get all the pkg-index attributes, then get the highest number and add one
    let pkgs = $(packed).map(function(x, value) { return +$(this).attr('pkg-index') }).toArray();
    let pkgCount = Math.max(...pkgs) + 1;

    while (this.packages.length < pkgCount)
    {
      //the vm.addPackage isn't firing, just click the button
      $('button[ng-click="vm.addPackage();"]').trigger('click').promise().done(function(e) { });
    }

    //loop the pkg count, get the commodities for that pkg, write the objects to the vm CommodityContents object
    for (let p = 0; p < pkgCount; p++)
    {
      let w = $.grep(this.working, function(item, i) { return item.packageIndex == p });
      this.packages[p].CommodityContents = w;
    }

    //click the General tab
    $('li[heading=General]:visible a').first().click();
    this.HideAssignGoodsPane();

    //after we are done, move back to the first package in the shipment
    while ($('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text() !== '1')
    {
      $('button[ng-click="vm.previousPackage();"]').first().click();
    }

  }

// GetNewCommodityObject(obj) // returns object
  GetNewCommodityObject(obj)
  {
    let c = {};

    Object.keys(obj).forEach(key =>
    {
      if (key != '$$hashKey' && key != 'packageIndex')
      {
        let value = obj[key];
        if (value) c[key] = value;
      }
    });

    return c;
  }

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
   this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
      var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
       shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference   = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
       shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = GetKeyValue('Custom2', originCustomData);
      // shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = "Ground";
   };

// function PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
   this.PreRate = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            var sfState = ConvertStateAbbr(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince);
            if (sfState !== null &&
                typeof sfState !== "undefined") {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince = sfState;
            }
        }
    };

// function GetKeyValue(key, arr) // returns string
  function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
      for (var index in arr) {
          if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
      }
      return '';
  }

// function ConvertStateAbbr(input) // returns string|undefined

        ['Montana', 'MT'],
        ['Nebraska', 'NE'],
        ['Nevada', 'NV'],
        ['New Hampshire', 'NH'],
        ['New Jersey', 'NJ'],
        ['New Mexico', 'NM'],
        ['New York', 'NY'],
        ['North Carolina', 'NC'],
        ['North Dakota', 'ND'],
        ['Northern Mariana Islands', 'NP'],
        ['Ohio', 'OH'],
        ['Oklahoma', 'OK'],
        ['Oregon', 'OR'],
        ['Pennsylvania', 'PA'],
        ['Puerto Rico', 'PR'],
        ['Rhode Island', 'RI'],
        ['South Carolina', 'SC'],
        ['South Dakota', 'SD'],
        ['Tennessee', 'TN'],
        ['Texas', 'TX'],
        ['US Virgin Islands', 'VI'],
        ['Utah', 'UT'],
        ['Vermont', 'VT'],
        ['Virginia', 'VA'],
        ['Washington', 'WA'],
        ['West Virginia', 'WV'],
        ['Wisconsin', 'WI'],
        ['Wyoming', 'WY'],
    ];

    input = input.replace(/\w\S*/g, function (txt) { return txt.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + txt.substr(1).toLowerCase(); });
    for (var state of states) {
        if (state[0] == input) {
            return (state[1]);
        }
    }

}

// function GetUserContext() // returns undefined
function GetUserContext() {
    if (userContext === undefined) {
        userContext = ajaxGet('api/usercontext/GET');
    }
}

// function ajaxGet(url) // returns result
function ajaxGet(url) {
    var result;
    $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: url,
        async: false,
        success: function(response) {
            result = response;
        }
    });
    return result;
}

this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        if(nameaddress.Code == "A1 - Ship to Buffalo" || nameaddress.Code == "A2 - Ship to Baltimore" || nameaddress.Code == "A3 - Ship to Harrisburg" || nameaddress.Code == "A4 - Millsboro Doc Image")
        {
            mailServiceShipment=true;
            var service = [{Symbol: "UPSAPI.UPS.NDAS", Name: "UPS Next Day Air Saver (UPS Adapter)"}];
            this.vm.profile.ProfileSetting.ServiceSelectionMode = 1;
            this.vm.selectedServices = service;
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount = 3;
            this.vm.showServiceSelection=true;
        }     
};

// GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) // returns string
this.GetCustom = function(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) {
    var returnValue = "";
    var customData = null;
    if (customDataType === "User") {
        if (shipmentRequest &&
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress &&
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData)
            customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
    }

    if (customData) {
        customData.forEach(function(customField) {
            if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
        });
    }
    return returnValue;

};

// Source: MarkenLLP (MLLP)_Inbound Returns CBR_EU_TO_UK_2498.cs
// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods');
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModal');

        //If the user profile is EU to UK, then Pickup LatestTimeReady can be calculated.
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 == "2") {

            //Storing the Number of Maximum labels in Misc Referene14.
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 = $('#Maxlabel').val();

            //Validating the maximum label count.
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == "" || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 % 1 !== 0) {
                alert("Maximum label count is invalid");
                throw new Error("Maximum label count is invalid");
            }
            else if (!(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 >= 1 && shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 <= 25)) {
                throw new Error("Number of labels needs to be a valid number between 1 and 25.");
            }
            
        }

    }

// function convertFileInputToBase64(inputId, leg) // returns Promise
    this.convertFileInputToBase64 = function (inputId, leg) {
        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {

            var data = {};
            const fileInput = $('#' + inputId);

            // Do not continue if there are no files
            if (!fileInput ||
                fileInput.length === 0 ||
                !fileInput[0].files ||
                fileInput[0].files.length === 0) {
                return;
            }

            // Get basic file info
            var file = fileInput[0].files[0];
            var fileName = file.name;

            // Create reader for reading files
            var reader = new FileReader();
            reader.readAsDataURL(file);
            reader.addEventListener("load", function () {

                // Create and return payload for upload call
                data = {
                    Action: "PaperlessDocUpload",
                    FileName: fileName,
                    encodedString: reader.result.split(',')[1],
                    shipperName: that.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper,
                    leg: leg
                }

                resolve(data);

            }, false);

            reader.addEventListener("error", function (error) {
                reject(error);
            }, false);

        });

    }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined; validates shipment contents before shipping
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        debugger;
        
       
        var i = 0, len = shipmentRequest.Packages.length;
        for (; i < len; i++) {
            var currentPackage = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
            debugger;
            if (currentPackage == null
                || currentPackage.CommodityContents == null
                || currentPackage.CommodityContents.length == 0) {
                var errorMsg = 'To obtain a UPS label to ship you must go to the Goods Tab above and process a paperless invoice for this shipment. Instructions on how to do this are located in your Starterpack.'
                console.log(errorMsg);
                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMsg);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
                throw Error(errorMsg);
            }
        }

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods');
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModal');
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined; initializes and converts shipment defaults and reference data
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {


        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;


        if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
        }

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();
        debugger;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 = "28454 Livingston Ave";
       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.City ="VALENCIA";
       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince ="CA";
       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company ="Dock 1 Specimen Processing";

       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Contact = "Q2 Solutions";

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country = "US";

       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PostalCode = "91355";
        
       shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Phone  = "9194052248";
         
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;
         
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

        //Storing StudyReference codes on the Miscreference17
        var studyReferenceCode = null;
        var studyReferenceCodeList = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations.length; i++) {
            
            studyReferenceCode = this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations[i].Value.split(',').map(x => x.trim());
            studyReferenceCodeList.push(studyReferenceCode);
        }
        var shipper = null;
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $("#OK").on("click", function () {
                debugger;
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val().trim();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if (arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)) {
                    var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue);
                    var selectedStudy = arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                    var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                    var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();

                    debugger;
                    var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                    var selectedSite = arrayOrders2[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();

                    //Assigning Shipper based on StudyReferenceCode available on validation list
                    for (var j = 0; j < studyReferenceCodeList.length; j++) {
                        var firstCode = studyReferenceCodeList[j];
                        if (firstCode.length >= 2 && firstCode[0] == selectedValue) {
                            shipper = "string:" + firstCode[1];
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(shipper);
                            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];


                        }
                    }

                }
                else {
                    alert("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                    throw new Error("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                }

                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                //GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest);

                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();

            });

        });

        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

    }

// this.convertFileInputToBase64(inputId, leg) // returns Promise resolving to upload payload object
this.convertFileInputToBase64 = function (inputId, leg) {
        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {

            var data = {};
            const fileInput = $('#' + inputId);

            // Do not continue if there are no files
            if (!fileInput ||
                fileInput.length === 0 ||
                !fileInput[0].files ||
                fileInput[0].files.length === 0) {
                return;
            }

            // Get basic file info
            var file = fileInput[0].files[0];
            var fileName = file.name;

            // Create reader for reading files
            var reader = new FileReader();
            reader.readAsDataURL(file);
            reader.addEventListener("load", function () {

                // Create and return payload for upload call
                data = {
                    Action: "PaperlessDocUpload",
                    FileName: fileName,
                    encodedString: reader.result.split(',')[1],
                    shipperName: that.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper,
                    leg: leg
                }

                resolve(data);

            }, false);

            reader.addEventListener("error", function (error) {
                reject(error);
            }, false);

        });

    }

// setCommodityDelegate() // returns undefined; validates and forces commodity quantity UOM selection
function setCommodityDelegate() {
        checkElmLoaded('[name="commoditiesModalForm"]').then((elm) => {
            debugger;
            const parentElm = elm;
            if (elm) {
                debugger;
                var footer = elm.querySelector('.modal-footer');
                if (footer) {
                    var saveButton = footer.querySelector('[value="Save"]');
                    if (saveButton) {
                        saveButton.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                            debugger;
                            var form = e.target.parentElement.parentElement;
                            var quantityUOM = form.querySelector('[ng-model="vm.commodityContent.QuantityUnitMeasure"]');
                            if (quantityUOM && quantityUOM.options) {
                                console.log('clicked');
                                var optionArray = Array.from(quantityUOM.options);

                                if (optionArray && optionArray.length > 0)
                                    var eachOption = optionArray.filter((x) => x.value == 'string:EA');
                                console.log('eachOption');
                                console.log(eachOption);
                                if (eachOption && eachOption.length == 1) {
                                    var indexOfEAOption = optionArray.indexOf(eachOption[0]);
                                    if (indexOfEAOption > 0) {
                                        quantityUOM.selectedIndex = indexOfEAOption;
                                        console.log('index');
                                        console.log(indexOfEAOption);
                                        quantityUOM.dispatchEvent(new window.Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                                        console.log('dispatched');
                                    }
                                }

                                debugger;
                                setTimeout(setCommodityDelegate, 500);
                            }

                            //that.vm.commodityContent.QuantityUnitMeasure = 'EA';
                        })
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

// setUploadDelegates() // returns undefined; sets upload handlers and validates file size before conversion
function setUploadDelegates() {

        debugger;
        setCommodityDelegate();

        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfModal', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfModalClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 'change');

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click', function (e) {

            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "true";

            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput[0].value = null;
            }
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";

            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            //debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', '');

            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
                if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                    uploadSuccessLabel.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    debugger;
                    that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                    $('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear').click();
                }
                else {

                    //debugger;
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 1, e).then(function (ret, e) {
                        //debugger;
                        //that.currentShipment.MiscReference19 = JSON.stringify(ret);
                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            //var test = this.setResponseLabel;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                            //debugger;
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfModal', 'click', function (e) {
            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfModalClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsModalInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsModalInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsModalInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsModalInput[0].value = null;
            }
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = "false";
            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', '');
            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabelModal = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');
                if (uploadSuccessLabelModal) {
                    uploadSuccessLabelModal.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    var test2 = that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                }
                else {
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 2).then(function (ret) {
                        //debugger;

                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName'));
                            //debugger;
                        }


                    });
                }
            }
        });

    };

// this.RepeatShipment(currentShipment) // returns undefined; resets shipment repeat defaults
this.RepeatShipment = function (currentShipment) {
        currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

    }

// Source: MarkenLLP (MLLP)_Inbound Returns CBR_US_TO_US_2499.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //Storing the Number of Maximum labels in Misc Referene14.
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 = $('#Maxlabel').val();
        //Validating the maximum label count.
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == "" || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 % 1 !== 0) {
            alert("Maximum label count is invalid");
            throw new Error("Maximum label count is invalid");
        }
        else if (!(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 >= 1 && shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 <= 25)) {
            throw new Error("Number of labels needs to be a valid number between 1 and 25.");
        }

    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
        }

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

        //Storing StudyReference codes on the Miscreference17
        var studyReferenceCode = null;
        var studyReferenceCodeList = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations.length; i++) {
            debugger;
            studyReferenceCode = this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations[i].Value.split(',').map(x => x.trim());
            studyReferenceCodeList.push(studyReferenceCode);
        }
        var shipper = null;
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $("#OK").on("click", function () {
                debugger;
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val().trim();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if (arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)) {
                    var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue);
                    var selectedStudy = arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                    var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                    var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();

                    var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                    var selectedSite = arrayOrders2[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();

                    //Assigning Shipper based on StudyReferenceCode available on validation list
                    for (var j = 0; j < studyReferenceCodeList.length; j++) {
                        var firstCode = studyReferenceCodeList[j];
                        if (firstCode.length >= 2 && firstCode[0] == selectedValue) {
                            shipper = "string:" + firstCode[1];
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(shipper);
                            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];


                        }
                    }

                }
                else {
                    alert("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                    throw new Error("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                }

                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                //GetUserShipper(selectedStudy,shipmentRequest);

                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();

            });

        });

        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

    }

// Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(inString, stringDelimiter) // returns array of non-empty trimmed string parts
            GetUniqueArrayFromString: function (inString, stringDelimiter = ',') {
                var trimArray = $.grep(inString.split(stringDelimiter), function (a) {
                    return a.trim().length > 0;
                });
                /* Get rid of any duplicate array entries. */
                //trimArray = trimArray.filter((e, i, a) => a.indexOf(e) === i);
                return trimArray;
            }

// Source: MarkenLLP (MLLP)_Marken_Phase2_CBR_2500.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //debugger;
        if (this.vm.profile.Name == "Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile") {
            //Setting Leg2 Company
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 == '') {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[3].Value;
            }

            //Setting Leg2 Shipper
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;
        }

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods');
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModal');
    }

// this.PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
this.PostShip = function (shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        //debugger;
        $('#Leg2LabelRequired').prop('checked', false);
        $('#DryIceRequired').prop('checked', false);
        $('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').prop('checked', false);
        $('#Leg2PackageWeight').val('');
        $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').val('');
        $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
        $('#quantity').val('');
        $('#EmptyPackaging').prop('checked', false);
        $('#displayMessage').hide();

        // Clear the upload error modal text
        $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html('');

        var userData1 = shipmentResponse.Packages[0].UserData1;
        var userData2 = shipmentResponse.Packages[0].UserData2;

        if (userData1) {
            var result = JSON.parse(userData1.replace(/'/g, '"'));
            //debugger;
            this.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', result);
        }

        if (userData2) {
            var result = JSON.parse(userData2.replace(/'/g, '"'));
            //debugger;
            this.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', result);
        }

    }

// this.setResponseLabel(responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) // returns void
this.setResponseLabel = function (responseLabelId, result, sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
        console.log("Upload Response: " + result);

        var label = $('#' + responseLabelId);
        if (label) {

            //debugger;

            if (sessionStorageErrorFileName) {
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + sessionStorageErrorFileName
                    + " - document exceeds maximum size (1.0 MB)";

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }

            else if (!result.Success) {
                // If the call is not successful, display an error message in a modal
                //debugger;
                var existingMessage = $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html();

                // Creates the error message
                var errorMessage = "Upload failed for document "
                    + result.FileName
                    + " during Leg "
                    + result.Leg
                    + ".";

                // If there is an existing error message, append to it
                if (existingMessage && existingMessage.length > 0) {
                    errorMessage = existingMessage + '<br /><br />' + errorMessage;
                }

                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMessage);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
            }
        }
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;

        //Declaring variables.
        var custom1_values, custom1, custom2, custom3, custom4, custom5, custom6, customData;
        var customValues = {};
        var customKeysArray = [];
        var CustomData_AfterCustom4 = [];
        var item;

        customData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
        // Iterate over the CustomData array and map values to their respective keys
        $.each(customData, function (index, item) {
            customValues[item.Key] = item.Value;
        });

        if (this.vm.profile.Name == 'Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile') {
            for (var i in customData.length) {
                item = customData[i];
                customKeysArray.push(item.Key);
            }

            var startIndex = -1;
            // Find the index of the key "Custom5"
            for (var i = 0; i < customData.length; i++) {
                if (customData[i].Key === "Custom5") {
                    startIndex = i;
                    break;
                }
            }

            // If "Custom5" is found, start storing values from it onwards
            if (startIndex !== -1) {
                for (var j = startIndex; j < customData.length; j++) {
                    CustomData_AfterCustom4.push(customData[j].Value);
                }
            }

            // Now, customValues object contains all custom values accessible by their keys
            var custom1 = customValues['Custom1'];
            var custom2 = customValues['Custom2'];
            var custom3 = customValues['Custom3'];
            var custom4 = customValues['Custom4'];
            var custom5 = customValues['Custom5'];
            var custom6 = customValues['Custom6'];
        } else {
            //debugger;
            custom1 = customValues['Custom1'];
            custom2 = customValues['Custom2'];
        }

        //Checking DryIceRequired sets true via User Custom1 data.
        if (custom1.split(',').length > 1) {
            custom1_values = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom1, ',');
        } else {
            throw new Error("Custom1 is not Comma delimited string.");
        }

        //Setting the Leg1Shipper
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = custom1_values[0];

        //Creating Dry Ice Required Checkbox
        if ($('#DryIceRequired').length == 0 && custom1_values[1] == "true") {
            //Adding DryIceRequired checkbox and its label.
            $('div.col-md-6:last').append($('<input />', {
                type: 'checkbox',
                id: 'DryIceRequired',
                name: 'DryIceRequired'
            }));
            $('div.col-md-6:last').append($('<label />', {
                for: 'DryIceRequired',
                text: 'Dry Ice Required'
            }));
        }

        //Comparing the User Custom2 with the Profile enabled Services and remove the unmatched services from the Service UI.
        var arrayValues_custom2;
        if (custom2 != null || custom2 != undefined) {
            arrayValues_custom2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom2, ',');
            var matchedValues = [];
            var profileServices = this.vm.profile.Services;
            profileServices.forEach(function (value1) {
                var serviceExists = arrayValues_custom2.some(function (value) {
                    return value1.Name.indexOf(value) !== -1;
                });
                if (serviceExists) {
                    matchedValues.push(value1);
                }
            });

            //Populating the Matched services on the Service UI.
            $(document).ready(function () {
                var mySelect = $('select[multiple="multiple"][property="Service"]');
                mySelect.empty(); //Clearing the existing Services listed out in the Service UI list.

                for (var i in matchedValues) {
                    mySelect.append($('<option></option>').attr('value', matchedValues[i].Symbol).text(matchedValues[i].Name));

                }
            });
        }

        //Retrieving Custom Data values after CustomData4(Leg2 Companies).
        var CustomDataCount = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData.length;

        var CustomData_FirstValues = []; //Fetch the First strings from Customdata after Custom4.
        var CustomData_OtherValues = []; //Fetch the rest of other strings from Customdata after Custom4.

        // Loop through each inner array in CustomData_AfterCustom4
        for (var i = 0; i < CustomData_AfterCustom4.length; i++) {

            var customData = CustomData_AfterCustom4[i];

            //var customData_values = customData.Value;

            var valuesArray = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(customData, ',');

            var firstValue = valuesArray.shift().trim();

            //Store the first string from the Custom data.
            CustomData_FirstValues.push(firstValue);

            //Store the remaining values
            CustomData_OtherValues.push(valuesArray.map(val => val.trim()));
        }


        //debugger;
        //Enabling the MiscReference1 field based on Profile.
        if (this.vm.profile.Name == "Outbound Labels Leg 2 Allowed User Profile") {

           // debugger;

            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide(); //When page loaded, MISCREFERENCE1 will be hidden.
                $('body').delegate('#DryIceRequired', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#DryIceRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        //debugger;
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').show();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "true";
                    } else {
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "false";
                    }
                });
            });

            $(document).ready(function () {
                if (custom1_values[2] == "true") {
                    $('#EmptyPackaging').hide();
                    $('label[for="EmptyPackaging"]').hide();
                }
                else {
                    $('#EmptyPackaging').show();
                    $('label[for="EmptyPackaging"]').show();
                }

            });

            //Creating Central Labs Frozen Sample Return Checkbox
            if ($('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').length == 0 && custom1_values[2] == "true") {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').addClass('inline-checkbox').append(
                    $('<input />').addClass('checkbox').attr({
                        'type': 'checkbox',
                        'id': 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn',
                        'name': 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn'
                    }),
                    $('<label />').attr('for', 'CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').text('Central Labs Frozen Samples Return')
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);

            }
            else {
                //Creating Empty Packaging Checkbox
                if ($('#EmptyPackaging').length == 0) {
                    //debugger;
                    var checkboxAndLabelContainer_Empty = $('<div>').addClass('inline-checkbox').append(
                        $('<input />').addClass('checkbox').attr({
                            'type': 'checkbox',
                            'id': 'EmptyPackaging',
                            'name': 'EmptyPackaging'
                        }),
                        $('<label />').attr('for', 'EmptyPackaging').text('Empty Packaging')
                    );

                    $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer_Empty);

                }



                //Setting MiscReference7 to true if Empty Packaging Checkbox is checked.
                $('body').delegate('#EmptyPackaging', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#EmptyPackaging').is(':checked')) {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = "true";
                    } else {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = "false";
                    }
                });
            }


            //Setting Leg2 Dry Ice weight hidden by default
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
                $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').hide();
            });
            //Setting MiscReference7 to true if Central Labs Frozen Sample Return Checkbox is checked.
            $('body').delegate('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn', 'change', function (e) {
                if ($('#CentralLabsFrozenSamplesReturn').is(':checked')) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = "true";

                    $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').show();
                    $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').show();

                } else {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = "false";
                    $('#Leg2DryIceWeight').hide();
                    $('label[for="Leg2DryIceWeight"]').hide();
                }
            });

            //Creating Leg2 Dry Ice Weight
            if ($('#Leg2DryIceWeight').length == 0) {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').append(
                    $('<label />').attr({
                        'for': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;top:120px;width:160px;'

                    }).text('Dry Ice Weight'),
                    $('<input />').attr({
                        'type': 'text',
                        'id': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'name': 'Leg2DryIceWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;border:1px solid black;top:140px;width:160px;'
                    }),
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);
            }

            //Setting MiscReference10 to true if Leg2 Dry Ice Weight is present.
            $('body').delegate('#Leg2DryIceWeight', 'change', function (e) {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference10 = $(this).val();
            });
            //Creating Leg2 Package Weight
            if ($('#Leg2PackageWeight').length == 0) {
                //debugger;
                var checkboxAndLabelContainer = $('<div>').append(
                    $('<label />').attr({
                        'for': 'Leg2PackageWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;top:70px;width:160px;'

                    }).text('Package Weight'),
                    $('<input />').attr({
                        'type': 'text',
                        'id': 'Leg2PackageWeight',
                        'name': 'Leg2PackageWeight',
                        'style': 'position:absolute;right:20px;border:1px solid black;top:90px;width:160px;'
                    }),
                );

                $('div.companyPopupModal').append(checkboxAndLabelContainer);
            }
            //debugger;
            //Setting MiscReference7 to true if Leg2 Package Weight is present.
            $('body').delegate('#Leg2PackageWeight', 'change', function (e) {
                //debugger;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference9 = $(this).val();
            });

            $('#divModalCompanyPopup').delegate('#Leg2PackageWeight', 'change', function (e) {
                //debugger;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference9 = $(this).val();
            });

            //Manual Upload
            var commodityLists = GetCommodityContents();
            $.each(commodityLists.CommodityContents, function (index, option) {
                var textMessage = commodityLists.CommodityContents[index].Description + ' ' + commodityLists.CommodityContents[index].HarmonizedCode;

                $('#commodityKey').append($('<option>', {
                    value: JSON.stringify(option),
                    text: textMessage
                }));
            });

            $('#addButton').one('click', function () {

                var showMessage = $('<div>').attr('id', 'displayMessage').text("Commodity added").css('font-weight', 'bold');
                $('.manualUpload').after(showMessage);

                var quantity = $('#quantity').val();
                if (quantity % 1 !== 0) {
                    alert("Qty is invalid");
                }
                else {
                    //Store Quantity in MiscReference15
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference15 = quantity;
                }

                //Store commodity content in Misc Reference14
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 = $('#commodityKey').val();
            });

            //Creating Service Dropdown if User Custom4 is present.
            var hasCustom4 = false;
            for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData.length; i++) {
                if (this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[i].Key === "Custom4") {
                    hasCustom4 = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (hasCustom4) {
                if (custom4 != '' && custom4 != 'undefined' && custom4 != null && $('#Service').length === 0) {
                    //Creating Service Dropdown menu.
                    var labelAndSelect1 = $('<label />').attr('for', 'Service').text('Service: ')
                        .add($('<select />').addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary').attr({
                            'id': 'Service',
                            'name': 'Service'
                        }).fadeIn());

                    $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend(labelAndSelect1);

                    var arrayOfValues_custom4 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom4, ',');

                    if (arrayOfValues_custom4.length > 1) {
                        $.each(arrayOfValues_custom4, function (i, e) {
                            $('#Service').append($('<option>', {
                                value: e,
                                text: e
                            }));
                        });

                        $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend($('<div />', {
                            'class': 'spacer'
                        }));

                    } else {
                        throw new Error("Custom4 is not comma-delimited.");
                    }
                }
            } else {
                alert("Custom4 is not present");
            }


            //Use case: 5 User Custom data fields -> Leg2 companies will be present only at the custom5 field.
            var CustomData5_FirstValues = [];
            var CustomData5_OtherValues = [];

            //if (CustomDataCount == 5) {
            //debugger;
            if ($('#Company').length === 0) {

                var custom5_Values = [];
                custom5_Values = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(custom5, ',');
                var custom5_firstValue = custom5_Values.shift().trim();

                //Store the first value
                CustomData5_FirstValues.push(custom5_firstValue);

                // Store the remaining values
                CustomData5_OtherValues.push(custom5_Values.map(val => val.trim()));
                //debugger;
                $('#CompanyName').val(custom5_Values[0]);
                $('#CompanyContact').val(custom5_Values[1]);
                $('#CompanyAddress').val(custom5_Values[2]);
                $('#CompanyCity').val(custom5_Values[3]);
                if (custom5_Values.Length > 7) {
                    //debugger;
                    $('#CompanyStateProvince').val(custom5_Values[4]);
                    $('#CompanyPostalCode').val(custom5_Values[5]);
                    $('#CompanyCountry').val(custom5_Values[6]);
                    $('#CompanyPhone').val(custom5_Values[7]);

                } else {
                    // debugger;
                    $('#CompanyStateProvince').val("");
                    $('#CompanyPostalCode').val(custom5_Values[4]);
                    $('#CompanyCountry').val(custom5_Values[5]);
                    $('#CompanyPhone').val(custom5_Values[6]);

                }

                $('body').delegate('#Leg2LabelRequired', 'change', this.vm, function (e) {
                    //debugger;
                    if ($('#Leg2LabelRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        //debugger;
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 = "true";
                        CompanyPopup.InitElements(function (selectedCompany, selectedService) {

                            //debugger;
                            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = CustomData5_OtherValues.toString();

                            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = selectedService;

                        });
                    }
                });
            }


            if ($('#Company').length === 0) {

                if ((custom5 != '' && custom5 != 'undefined' && custom5 != null) && (custom6 != '' && custom6 != 'undefined' && custom6 != null)) {
                    //Creating Company Dropdown menu.
                    var labelAndSelect = $('<label />').attr('for', 'Company').text('Company: ')
                        .add($('<select />').addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary').attr({
                            'id': 'Company',
                            'name': 'Company'
                        }).fadeIn());

                    //$('div.modal-body').prepend(labelAndSelect);
                    $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend(labelAndSelect);



                    $.each(CustomData_FirstValues, function (i, e) {
                        $('#Company').append($('<option>', {
                            value: e,
                            text: e
                        }));
                    });

                    $('div.companyPopupModal').prepend($('<div />', {
                        'class': 'spacer' // Ensure you define this class in your CSS with the desired spacing
                    }));

                    // Event listener for company selection change
                    $('body').delegate('#Company', 'change', function (e) {
                        //debugger;
                        var selectedCompany = $(this).find(":selected").val();
                        CompanyPopup.populateCorrespondingValues(selectedCompany, CustomData_FirstValues, CustomData_OtherValues);
                    });

                    // Trigger change event on company dropdown to populate corresponding values by default
                    $('#Company').trigger('change');

                }

                //If Leg2LabelRequired check box is checked, setting MiscReference6 to true and populating the Company and Service values on the Modal.
                $('body').delegate('#Leg2LabelRequired', 'change', this.vm, function (e) {
                    if ($('#Leg2LabelRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6 = "true";

                        if ((custom4 != '' || custom4 != 'undefined' || custom4 != null) || (custom5 != '' || custom5 != 'undefined' || custom5 != null) && (custom6 != '' || custom6 != 'undefined' || custom6 != null)) {

                            CompanyPopup.InitElements(function (selectedCompany, selectedService) {

                                var com = CompanyPopup.populateCorrespondingValues(selectedCompany, CustomData_FirstValues, CustomData_OtherValues);

                                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = com.toString();
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = selectedService;

                            });
                            $("#buttonCompanyPopup").click();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }

            //debugger;
            //Setting Leg1 and Leg2 PDF Invoice default by False.         
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = "false";


        } else {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide(); //When page loaded, MISCREFERENCE1 will be hidden.
                $('body').delegate('#DryIceRequired', 'change', function (e) {
                    if ($('#DryIceRequired').is(':checked')) {
                        //debugger;
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').show();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "true";

                    } else {
                        $('[property="MiscReference1"]').hide();
                        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = "false";
                    }
                });
            });

            //Setting Leg1 PDF Invoice default by False
            //debugger;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";

        }
        //debugger;
        //Assigning the User address to Return Address
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;
        //this.vm.profile.Shippers= this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        //Assigning the Weight Units to "KG" if Ship From country is not US.
        //debugger;
        var selectedShipper = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper; //$('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val();
        var map = $.grep(this.vm.profile.Shippers, function (shipper) {
            console.log(shipper.Symbol);
            return shipper.Symbol == selectedShipper;
        })[0];
        if (map.Country != "US") {
            //debugger;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Units = "KG";
        }
        
        
         //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    
                     var total=0;
                for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                    total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                }
                var inst=[];
                inst.push(total);
                debugger;
				shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions=inst[0].toString();
               
                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });
        
    }

// this.convertFileInputToBase64(inputId, leg) // returns Promise resolving to upload payload object or undefined
this.convertFileInputToBase64 = function (inputId, leg) {
        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {

            var data = {};
            const fileInput = $('#' + inputId);

            // Do not continue if there are no files
            if (!fileInput ||
                fileInput.length === 0 ||
                !fileInput[0].files ||
                fileInput[0].files.length === 0) {
                return;
            }

            // Get basic file info
            var file = fileInput[0].files[0];
            var fileName = file.name;

            // Create reader for reading files
            var reader = new FileReader();
            reader.readAsDataURL(file);
            reader.addEventListener("load", function () {

                // Create and return payload for upload call
                data = {
                    Action: "PaperlessDocUpload",
                    FileName: fileName,
                    encodedString: reader.result.split(',')[1],
                    shipperName: that.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper,
                    leg: leg
                }

                resolve(data);

            }, false);

            reader.addEventListener("error", function (error) {
                reject(error);
            }, false);

        });

    }

// function setUploadDelegates() // returns void
function setUploadDelegates() {

        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfModal', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#btnUploadPdfModalClear', 'click');
        $('body').undelegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 'change');

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoods', 'click', function (e) {
            //debugger;
            //that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "true";

            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput[0].value = null;
            }
            //debugger;
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "false";

            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            //debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', '');

            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabel');
                if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                    uploadSuccessLabel.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                    $('#btnUploadPdfGoodsClear').click();
                }
                else {
                    that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = "true";
                    //debugger;
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputGoods', 1, e).then(function (ret, e) {
                        //debugger;
                        //that.currentShipment.MiscReference19 = JSON.stringify(ret);
                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfModal', 'click', function (e) {
            // Simply clicks on the file input (hidden from user) to open the file chooser dialog
            var uploadPDFGoodsInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsInput) {
                uploadPDFGoodsInput.trigger('click');
            }

        });

        $('body').delegate('#btnUploadPdfModalClear', 'click', function (e) {
            var uploadPDFGoodsModalInput = $('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal');
            if (uploadPDFGoodsModalInput
                && uploadPDFGoodsModalInput.length == 1) {
                uploadPDFGoodsModalInput[0].value = null;
            }
            that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = "false";
            var uploadSuccessLabel = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');
            if (uploadSuccessLabel) {
                uploadSuccessLabel.text("No file selected");
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 'change', function (e) {
            // Ensures that a file is present before continuing
            //debugger;
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', '');
            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', '');
            if (e &&
                e.target &&
                e.target.files &&
                e.target.files.length > 0) {

                sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName', e.target.files[0].name);

                var uploadSuccessLabelModal = $('#uploadSuccessLabelModal');
                if (uploadSuccessLabelModal) {
                    uploadSuccessLabelModal.text("Invoice to upload selected: " + e.target.files[0].name);
                }

                if (e.target.files[0].size > 1000000) {
                    var test2 = that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoodsFileName'));
                    $('#btnUploadPdfModalClear').click();
                }
                else {
                    that.convertFileInputToBase64('paperlessUploadFileInputModal', 2).then(function (ret) {
                        //debugger;

                        that.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference12 = "true";

                        try {
                            sessionStorage.setItem('uploadDocumentDataModal', JSON.stringify(ret));
                        } catch (err) {
                            //debugger;
                            that.setResponseLabel('uploadSuccessLabel', {}, sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModalFileName'));
                            //debugger;
                        }



                    });
                }
            }
        });

    }
