// setCurrencyOptions(list, element) // returns void
function setCurrencyOptions(list, element)
    {
        var interval = setInterval(function() 
            {
                var currencies = $(element);
                if (currencies.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function(){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
    }

// replaceOptionValues(list, element) // returns void
function replaceOptionValues(list, element) {
        var valuelist = list.map(function (e) { return 'string:' + e });
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
            var $element = $(element);
            if ($element.length) {
                clearInterval(interval);
                $element.each(function () {
                    if (!valuelist.includes(this.value) && this.value != '') this.remove();
                });
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {

    //debugger;

    //Map Store Number to ShipperReference
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = nameaddress.Code;

    //Set Default Services Based on From and To Countries		
    var fromCountry = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country;
    var toCountry = nameaddress.Country;

    //Email Address Mappings
	if(nameaddress.Email != null)
	{
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
	}

    //Store Address Book ID value in MiscReference20 to signify that consignee address came from Address Book and was not manually entered.
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = nameaddress.AddressBookId.toString();


    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.GND")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}
}

// SetSelectedService(serviceSymbol) // returns void
this.SetSelectedService = function(serviceSymbol)
    {
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.Services.length; i++)
        {
            if (this.vm.profile.Services[i].Symbol === serviceSymbol)
            {
                this.vm.selectedServices = [this.vm.profile.Services[i]];
                this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = this.vm.profile.Services[i];
                break;
            }
        }
    }
}

// SetCurrencyCAD(shipToCountry) // returns void
this.SetCurrencyCAD = function(shipToCountry)
{
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        if (shipToCountry === "CA")
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
        }
        else
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "USD" };
        }
    }
}

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //debugger;
        var shipperSymbol = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper;

        //Skip Ship Goods Type Selection for these international shipper origins
        if (shipperSymbol != "SEGONZAC_FR" && shipperSymbol != "SURREY_UK" && shipperSymbol != "DUBLIN_IE" && shipperSymbol != "NAYANDA_IN" && shipperSymbol != "FRANKFORT_RETURNS") {
            var shipGoodsType = document.getElementById('ship_goods_type').options[document.getElementById('ship_goods_type').selectedIndex].value;
            var pkg1MiscRef4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
            //if (shipGoodsType == null || shipGoodsType == 'undefined' || shipGoodsType == '' || shipGoodsType == 'default')
            if (pkg1MiscRef4 == null || pkg1MiscRef4 == undefined || pkg1MiscRef4 == '' || shipGoodsType == 'default') {
                $("#ship_goods_type").val('default');
                //$('#ship_goods_type').css('background-color', '#FF3333');
                $('#ship_goods_type').focus();
                var errorMessage = "Error, You must select a Shipment Goods Type on the first package of the shipment";
                alert(errorMessage);
                return;
            }
        }

        //#region Require Field Validation
        if (shipperSymbol != "FRANKFORT_RETURNS") {
            //debugger;
            //var costCodeValue = $("#ctl00_cphContent_right_tabs_ref_tab_ref_ctrl_misc_ref_pane_content_misc_reference_3_txt").val();
            var costCodeValue = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
            if (costCodeValue == null || costCodeValue == undefined || costCodeValue == '') {
                $('#costcodes').focus();
                var errorMessage = "Error, You must select a Cost Code value on the first package of the shipment";
                alert(errorMessage);
            }
        }
        //#endregion

        var thirdParty = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference19;
        var adultSignature = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference20;

        userParams.third_party_rule = thirdParty;
        userParams.adult_signature_required_rule = adultSignature;
    };

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
    this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
        //#region Package Details
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].description;
        //#endregion

        //#region Reference
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference5 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5;
        //#endregion

        //#region User Data
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].UserData1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData1;
        //#endregion

        //#region Email Notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipNotificationEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationEmail;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationEmail;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;
        //#endregion

        //#region Get Scale Weight
        //get_weight_scale_btn_OnClick();
        if (vmTemp && vmTemp.profile.ScaleConfiguration !== undefined) {    // get Weight if button isn't disabled
			vmTemp.getWeight();
		}
        //#endregion
    };

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void; validates shipper reference before shipping
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        var shipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        if (!this.vm.IsValid('ShipperReference', shipperReference)) {
            throw ({ message: "Cost Center is invalid [" + shipperReference + "].", errorCode: "001" });
        }
    };

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void; converts and validates shipment data
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.IsValid = this.IsValidated;
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);

        if (!this.vm.IsValid('ShipperReference', shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference)) {
            throw ({ message: 'Cost Center is invalid from User Custom Data', errorCode: '001' });
        }

        if (pageLoaded) {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = consigneeStateIsRequired;
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = consigneePhoneIsRequired
            vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = descriptionIsRequired;
        }
    };

// this.IsValidated(referenceField, referenceValue) // returns boolean; validates a reference value against field options
    this.IsValidated = function (referenceField, referenceValue) {
        var isValid = false;
        if (this.fieldOptions[referenceField]) {
            var options = this.fieldOptions[referenceField].FieldOptionValidations;
            options.forEach(function (option) {
                if (option.Value.trim() === referenceValue.trim()) isValid = true;
            });
        }
        //if (referenceValue.length === 0 || !referenceValue.trim()) isValid = false;
        return isValid;
    };

// CreateOrderTable(OrderJson) // returns void
  CreateOrderTable = (OrderJson) =>
  {
    //empty any current table rows
    this.M.Table.Empty();

    //slide the panel up
    this.M.LeftPanel.Toggle();

    //fill the table with the incoming data, prepared by the DynamicHtml class
    this.M.Table.Fill(new DynamicHtml().GetNewTableMarkup(OrderJson))

    //slide the panel down
    this.M.LeftPanel.Toggle();

    //calculate the total items in the order and store the value
    this.Items.Ordered = OrderJson.reduce((a, b) => +a + +b.forderqty, 0);
    this.Items.Remaining = this.Items.Ordered;

    //initialize the tooltips
    $(this.H.TableId).find('[data-toggle=tooltip]').tooltip();

    //update the total ordered badge
    $(this.H.OrderedItemsCount).text(this.Items.Ordered);
  }

// GetNewTableMarkup(OrderData) // returns array of table row elements
  GetNewTableMarkup = (OrderData) =>
  {
    let that = this, rows = [];
    const json = new JsonData();

    //loop through the data and create the object that will be attached to each row as a .data() object
    OrderData.forEach((item, index) =>
    {
      json.TrimAllKeysAndValues(OrderData);

      //setup the row data object
      let data = {};
      //the .Count var is used when the items get placed into containers, it represents the count of items in the parent container object
      data.Count = 0;
      data.ItemNumber = item.CSpartno;
      data.ItemDescription = item.CSdescript;
      data.HarmonizedCode = (item.CSHTScode || 'Not Available');
      data.HarmonizedDescription = (item.CSHTSDESC || 'Not Available');
      data.CountryOfOrigin = (item.CSCOO || 'Not Available');
      data.OrderNumber = item.CSsono;
      data.OrderRevision = item.CSsorev;
      data.OrderString = item.CSsono + ` (${item.CSsorev})`;
      data.PurchaseOrder = item.fcustpono;
      data.QuantityOrdered = +item.CSshITMqty;
      data.QuantityPacked = 0;
      data.QuantityRemaining = +item.CSshITMqty;
      data.RowId = (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
      data.RowIndex = index;
      data.PackedItems = []; //.PackedItems will be {} objects with a structure of .ContainerIndex = x, .Count = y

      let row = $('tr.table-row-template').clone()
        .removeClass('table-row-template')
        .attr('row-id', data.RowId)
        .data(data);

      //add all the data to the table row
      $(row).find('td').each(function(i, td)
      {
        let key = $(td).attr('sos-key');
        $(td).find('div:first').text(data[key]);
      });

      //setup the tooltip for the description
      let title = `<div class="text-left"><span>HTS: <b>${data.HarmonizedCode}</b></span><br/>`;
      title += `<span>C/O: <b>${data.CountryOfOrigin}</b></span></div>`;
      $(row).find('td.item-description').first().attr({ 'data-toggle': "tooltip", 'data-placement': 'top', 'data-html': 'true', 'data-container': 'body', 'title': title });

      rows.push(row);
    });

    return rows;
  }

// AddItemDataToContainer(row, qty, ci) // returns void
  AddItemDataToContainer = (row, qty, ci) =>
  {
    const msg = {};
    try
    {
      if (row.QuantityRemaining == 0) throw 'Item completely packed.';

      //if the user passed in an integer, use that, otherwise, use 1
      qty = qty || 1;

      //increment the number of items packed
      row.QuantityPacked += qty;
      row.QuantityRemaining -= qty;
      const ContainerIndex = +(ci || this.Containers.Active);

      //get a reference to the global container data
      let globalContainer = this.Containers.List.filter(c => c.ContainerIndex == ContainerIndex)[0];
      globalContainer.ItemCount += qty;

      //update the global root Containers object as well
      this.Containers.ItemCount += qty;

      const bExists = this.DataStore.TableRowPackedItemCount(row.RowId, ContainerIndex);

      //the item has no entries in the current container, create a new entry in the .PackedItems array
      //and then create a new list item to add to the current container
      if (!bExists)
      {
        //add the item to the global object
        //do this before the .PackedItems get added to the row as we don't need/want that object
        let p = {};
        Object.keys(row).forEach((val) => { if (val !== 'PackedItems') { p[val] = row[val]; } })
        globalContainer.Items.push(p);

        //add the packed item to the row .data() object
        let container = {};
        container.ContainerIndex = ContainerIndex;
        container.Count = 0;
        row.PackedItems.push(container);

        //add the list item to the active container
        this.AddItemHtmlToContainer(new DynamicHtml().GetNewListItemMarkup(row, ContainerIndex), ContainerIndex);
      }

      //increment the global var with the total number of items packed
      this.Items.Packed += qty;
      this.Items.Remaining -= qty;

      //increment the table row .data() var
      let item = this.DataStore.TableRowPackedItems(row.RowId, ContainerIndex);
      item.Count += qty;

      let globalItem = globalContainer.Items.filter(i => i.RowId == row.RowId)[0];
      //update the global containers
      globalItem.Count += +qty;
      //try to remove other containers from .PackedItems
      //globalItem.PackedItems = globalItem.PackedItems.filter(f => f.ContainerIndex == ContainerIndex);

      //make sure the list item and the row item have matching .data() objects
      //as of jQuery 1.4+ the .data() object can only be copied with a shallow merge so remove and recreate here
      this.SyncDataObjects(row.RowId);

      msg.Action = 'AddItem';
      msg.ContainerIndex = ContainerIndex;
      msg.ItemNumber = row.ItemNumber;

      this.UpdateToastNotification(msg);

      this.UpdateScreenElements();
    }
    catch (error)
    {
      msg.Action = 'Error';
      msg.ErrorMessage = error;
      this.UpdateToastNotification(msg);
    }
  }

// RemoveItemDataFromContainer(RowId, Quantity, ContainerIndex) // returns void
  RemoveItemDataFromContainer = (RowId, Quantity, ContainerIndex) =>
  {
    const msg = {};
    ContainerIndex = (ContainerIndex || this.Containers.Active)
    try
    {
      Quantity = Quantity || 1;

      //get a reference to the global container data
      let globalContainer = this.Containers.List.filter(c => c.ContainerIndex == ContainerIndex)[0];
      globalContainer.ItemCount -= Quantity;

      //update the global Containers root object with a cumulative total
      this.Containers.ItemCount -= Quantity;

      //get the matching table row, update the object, then copy the .data() to the list item
      let row = this.DataStore.TableRowDataObject(RowId);
      row.QuantityPacked -= Quantity;
      row.QuantityRemaining += Quantity;

      let packedItems = this.DataStore.TableRowPackedItems(RowId, ContainerIndex);
      packedItems.Count -= Quantity;

      //if there are no more of this row of items packed in the container, remove the list item
      //and update the containers array
      if (packedItems.Count === 0)
      {
        //remove the list item from view
        this.RemoveItemHtmlFromContainer(RowId);

        //remove the item from the global containers object
        globalContainer.Items = globalContainer.Items.filter(f => f.RowId !== RowId);
      }

      //update the global var
      this.Items.Packed -= Quantity;
      this.Items.Remaining += Quantity;

      //make sure the list item and the row item have matching .data() objects
      //as of jQuery 1.4+ the .data() object can only be copied with a shallow merge so remove and recreate here
      this.SyncDataObjects(RowId);

      this.UpdateScreenElements();

      msg.Action = 'RemoveItem';
      msg.ContainerIndex = ContainerIndex;
      msg.ItemNumber = row.ItemNumber;

      this.UpdateToastNotification(msg);
    }
    catch (error)
    {
      console.log(error);
      msg.Action = 'Error';
      msg.ErrorMessage = error.message;
      this.UpdateToastNotification(msg);
    }
  }

// function PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) 
    {               
        loadselectedValue=loadValue;
        // Converting JS object to an array
        shipmentRequestObject =  JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest));
        
        ChromeScrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);

        // Check for not found error
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(0,1) == '~')    
                {
                 alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(1));
				  $("input:text").eq(0).focus();   
			  this.vm.newShipment();
	       		return;
                }
        }
        
        //Send OSCO related errors to end user
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if (window.confirm(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20 + "\nContinue with shipment?")) 
            {
              //alert("You pressed OK");
            } 
            else 
            {
                $("input:text").eq(0).focus();
            }   
        }
      
        // Check for address validation required
        if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4 == 'Y')    
                {
                var interval = setInterval(function() {
                const consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                consigneeCompany = consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Company"]');
                consigneePostalCode = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="postalCode"]');
                consigneeCity = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                consigneeState = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');

                var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && consigneePostalCode.length && consigneeCity.length && consigneeState.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] button[title="Validate Address"]').click();                    
                    }
                }, 50);
            }
        }
  
        $('[name="address1"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1);
        
        $('[name="company"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company);
        
    //debugger;
    }

// function DrawDataInReturnForm() // returns void
function DrawDataInReturnForm(){
        var carrierEmailReturnLabelMethod = 5;
        $('form[name="returnForm"]').find('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val(RETURN_DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION);
        $('form[name="returnForm"]').find('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]').prop("checked", true);
        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]>option:eq('+ carrierEmailReturnLabelMethod +')').prop('selected', true);
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val(shipmentRequestObject.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);
    }

// function MarkShipmentAsReturn() // returns void
function MarkShipmentAsReturn(){
        for (let i = 0; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++) 
        {
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDelivery = true;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = shipmentRequestObject.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Description = RETURN_DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION;             
        }
    }

// function UnMarkShipmentAsReturn() // returns void
function UnMarkShipmentAsReturn(){
        for (let i = 0; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++) 
        {
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDelivery = false;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryMethod = undefined;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = '';
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Description = '';
        }
    }

// function ClearAllInputFields() // returns void
function ClearAllInputFields()
    {
        var loadedOrderValue = $('input[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').val();
        var elements = document.getElementsByTagName("input");        
        for (var ii=0; ii < elements.length; ii++) 
        {
            if (elements[ii].type == "text" && elements[ii].value != loadedOrderValue) 
            {
                elements[ii].value = "";
            }
        }  
        
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]').prop("checked", false);
        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]>option:eq(0)').prop('selected', true)
        $('textarea[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val();
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val();
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmailLocale"]').val();
         shipmentRequestObject =  {}
    }

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        var originCustomData = GetCustomData(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress);        
        //shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData);
        //shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Origin = GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData);

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = GetKeyValue('TMID', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = GetKeyValue('ENTITY', originCustomData);        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = GetKeyValue('GL_CODE', originCustomData);                
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = GetKeyValue('DEPARTMENT', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Code = GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData);
        
        var location = GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData);
        
        // MOS or MOO to switch shipper to main office 
        if(location == "MOS" || location == "MOO")
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "MOS";
    };

// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
    debugger;
    var consolidatedOpportunities = $("#txtConsolidatedFields").find('*').filter(':input:visible:first').val();
    
       if ($("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked") && ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities))
       {
         var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("true",consolidatedOpportunities,loadValue);
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession;
       }
       else
       {
            var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("false","",loadValue);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession
       }
    }

// function ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities) // returns boolean
    function ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities)
    {
        var rexVal = /^[A-Z0-9]+((,|-)[A-Z0-9]+)*[A-Z0-9]+$/;
        var result = true;
        if (!rexVal.test(consolidatedOpportunities.toUpperCase()))
        {
            if (consolidatedOpportunities.trim()==="")
            {
                result=true;
            }
            else
            {
                alert("Consolidated opportunities not well formed.");
                result= false;
            }
        }
        return result;
    }

// function CreateShippingSession(IsConsolidatedShipping, ConsolidatedOpportunities, OpportunityLoaded) // returns string
    function CreateShippingSession(IsConsolidatedShipping,ConsolidatedOpportunities,OpportunityLoaded)
    {
        var jsonObject = {};
        jsonObject["IsConsolidatedShipping"] = IsConsolidatedShipping;
        jsonObject["ConsolidatedOpportunities"] = ConsolidatedOpportunities.split(',');
        jsonObject["OpportunityLoaded"] = OpportunityLoaded;
        return JSON.stringify(jsonObject);
    }

// Source: Target (TARGET)_Target CBR_2489.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined; throws ValidationError if MiscReference1 is missing or blank
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
        if (!shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1.trim() === '') {
            // Highlight the field if it has no value
            waitForInputs();    

            const err = new Error('MiscReference1 is required');
            err.name = 'ValidationError'; // Optional custom name
            err.code = 'MISC_REF_001';    // Custom property
            throw err;
        } else {
            const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('[ng-model*="MiscReference1"]');
            if (inputs.length > 0) {
                inputs.forEach(input => {
                    input.style.border = null;
                });
            }
        }

        function waitForInputs() {
            const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
            const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('[ng-model$="MiscReference1"]');
            if (inputs.length > 0) {
                inputs.forEach(input => {
                input.style.border = '1px solid red';
                });
                observer.disconnect(); // stop watchin
            }
            });

            observer.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });

        }
    }

// Source: The Home Depot (HOMEDEPOT)_New CBR 2026_2508.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void; validates return-label selection and consignee phone requirements
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        if (this.vm.returnLabel && this.vm.GTSreturnLabel) {
            throw Error('You have selected to include a Return Label AND Global Tech Return Label. Please un-check one or the other and try again.');
        }

        if (this.vm.returnLabel || this.vm.GTSreturnLabel) {
            if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Phone === null ||
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Phone === '') {
                {
                    throw Error('You selected to print a return label but you did not provide the consignee phone number.');
                }
            }
        }
    }

// this.PostalCodeLookup(addressName) // returns void; looks up postal code and validates/updates city and state
    this.PostalCodeLookup = function (addressName) {
        var userContext = this.getUserContext(this);
        var postalCode = $('[address-property-name="' + addressName + '"] [name="postalCode"]').val();
        var content = { AddressName: addressName, PostalCode: postalCode };
        var payload = { Action: 'CSZ', Content: JSON.stringify(content) };
        var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(payload), UserContext: userContext };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).responseJSON;
        if (response.ErrorCode > 0) {
            client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', response.ErrorMessage)
        } else {
            var responseData = JSON.parse(client.htmlText(response.Data));
            if (responseData === null) {
                client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', 'Invalid or Not US Postal Code');
            } else {
                if (responseData.length > 1) {
                    this.addressResults = responseData;
                    client.shipping.validateAddressModalShow();
                } else {
                    this.currentShipment.updateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, responseData[0].City, responseData[0].StateProvince)
                }
            }
        }
    }

// this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, city, stateProvince) // returns void; updates address city/state and country based on province
    this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ = function (addressName, city, stateProvince) {
        var nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (addressName == 'ReturnAddress') {
            if (this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress === undefined)
                this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {};
            nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress;
        }
        nameAddress.City = city;
        nameAddress.StateProvince = stateProvince;

        if (stateProvince == 'PR') {
            nameAddress.Country = 'PR';
        }
        else {
            nameAddress.Country = 'US';
        }
    }

// this.SelectAddress(address) // returns void; applies selected validated address to shipment
    this.SelectAddress = function (address) {
        client.shipping.validateAddressModalHide();
        this.updateNameAddressCSZ(address.AddressName, address.City, address.StateProvince);
    }

// PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;

        var shipToEmail = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);
        var shipFromEmail = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Email);
        var ref1 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1);
        var ref2 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2);
        var ref3 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
        var ref4 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4);
        var ref5 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5);
        var ref6 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6);
        var ref7 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7);
        var ref8 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8);

        var shipperRef = ref1 + "~" + ref2 + "~" + ref3 + "~" + ref4;
        var consigneeRef = ref5 + "~" + ref6;//ref7 + "~" + ref8 + "~" +

        shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg)
        {
            if(pkg.MiscReference7)
            {
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages.length > 1 ) {
                    throw ({message: 'Multiple Packages Not Support with Dry Ice', errorCode: ''});
                }

                if (returnPropertyValue(pkg.MiscReference8) === '')
                {
                    throw ({message: 'Missing Dry Ice Weight', errorCode: ''});
                }
                
                var ret = ref8;
                
                var DryIceWeight = {
                    "Amount": ret.replace('kgs',''),
                    "Units": "KG"
                };
				pkg.DryIceWeight = DryIceWeight;
				
				var Country = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country;
				console.log(Country);
				if(Country =="US"){
				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 1;
				}else{
				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 2;
				}
                pkg.DryIcePurpose = 2;
            }
            pkg.ShipperReference = shipperRef;
            pkg.ConsigneeReference = consigneeRef;
            pkg.MiscReference20 = userContext.UserId;

            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = '';
            pkg.ShipNotificationEmail = shipToEmail != '' || shipFromEmail != '';
            if (shipToEmail != '') {
                pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipToEmail;
            }

            if (shipFromEmail != '' ) {
                if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + shipFromEmail;
                } else {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipFromEmail;
                }
            }
        });
    }

// setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement() // returns void
    function setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement() {
        var isRequired = vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country == 'US';
        if (!isRequired) {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = false;
        } else {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = consigneeStateIsRequired;
        }
    }

// function IsValid(referenceField, referenceValue) // returns boolean
        IsValid(referenceField, referenceValue) {
            var isValid = false;
            if (this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField]) {
                var options = this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField].FieldOptionValidations
                options.forEach(function (option) {
                    if (option.Value.trim() === referenceValue.trim()) isValid = true;
                });
            }

            if (referenceValue.length === 0 || !referenceValue.trim()) isValid = false;
            return isValid;
        }

// function validationCVIS(Type) // returns void
function validationCVIS(Type){
        var Shipper = $("#CVIS_Shippers").val();
        if(Shipper === "0"){
            client.alert.Danger("Select a valid Shipper");
        }else{
            var TrailerSortCode = $("#TrailerSortCode").val();
            if(TrailerSortCode === ""){
                client.alert.Danger("No Trailer Sort Code found for Shipper "+ Shipper);
            }else{
                //AllGood
                execCvisAction(Type);
            }
        }
       
    }

// function CloseReal() // returns void
function CloseReal(){
	    var Shipper = $("#CVIS_Shippers").val();
        var TrailerNumber = $("#TrailerNumber").val();
		var percentageComplete = $("#percentageComplete").val();
		if(percentageComplete === null || percentageComplete === ""){
		    client.alert.Danger("Percentage Complete is required")
		    return;
		}
        var usermethodParams = { "action": 8, "orderNumber": "0", "percentageComplete":percentageComplete, "trailerNumber":TrailerNumber, "shipper":Shipper};
    	
		var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
		var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
			if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
				client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
			} else {
				client.alert.Info(response.Data);
                if(response.Data === "Success"){
                    CloseModalClose();
                    getTrailerSortCodeByShipper();
                    $("#TrailerNumber").val("");
                }
			}
		});
		
		/*$.ajax({
        type: "POST",
            url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            dataType: "json",
            data: { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) },
            success: function(response) {
                alert(response.Data);
                if(response.Data === "Success"){
                    CloseModalClose();
                    getTrailerSortCodeByShipper();
                    $("#TrailerNumber").val("");
                }
                
            },
            error: function (error) {
                alert(error);
            }
        });*/
	}

// function UserMethod(logoNumber) // returns void
function UserMethod(logoNumber) {

		if (logoNumber == 4) {

			var orderNumber = $('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').val();

			if (orderNumber === undefined || orderNumber === null || orderNumber === "") {

				client.alert.Danger("Missing or invalid Order Number, no update made.  Please enter a valid order number and try again.");
			}
			else {
			
				var usermethodParams = { "action": 4, "orderNumber": orderNumber, "percentageComplete":"0", "trailerNumber":"", "shipper":""};
				var results;
				var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
				var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
					if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
						client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
					} else {
						results = response["Data"];
					}
				});

                        ;
                    },
                    error: function (error) {
                        alert("Finalize Shipment has failed, no update made to the system.  Contact Support.");
                    }
                });*/
			}
		}
		else {

			$("#fileLoader").click();

			var encodedBase64Logo;

			var filesSelected = document.getElementById("fileLoader").files;

			if (filesSelected.length > 0) {
				var fileToLoad = filesSelected[0];

				var fileReader = new FileReader();

				fileReader.readAsDataURL(fileToLoad);

				fileReader.onload = function (event) {
					var encodedBase64Logo = logoNumber + event.target.result;

					SoxOnWcfDblHop.userMethod(encodedBase64Logo,
						function (result) {
							// Do something with the data

							DisplayLogoSaveMessage(result);

						},
						function (e) {
							// Do something with the error

							alert(e.message);
						});
				};
			}
		}
	}

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    var consigneeCode = $('select[ng-model="xConsigneeCode"]');
    var selectCode = consigneeCode.val().substring(7);

    if (selectCode === '')
    {
      throw ({ message: 'Please select a lab', errorCode: 43770 });
    }
    var arr = this.vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes;
    var obj = arr.filter(function(nameaddress)
    {
      if (nameaddress.Code === selectCode) { return nameaddress; }
    });

    if (obj.length)
    {
      var nameaddress = obj[0];
      var consignee = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
      consignee.Company = nameaddress.Company;
      consignee.Contact = nameaddress.Contact;
      consignee.Address1 = nameaddress.Address1;
      consignee.Address2 = nameaddress.Address2;
      consignee.Address3 = nameaddress.Address3;
      consignee.City = nameaddress.City;
      consignee.StateProvince = nameaddress.StateProvince;
      consignee.PostalCode = nameaddress.PostalCode;
      consignee.Country = nameaddress.Country;
      consignee.Phone = nameaddress.Phone;
      consignee.Email = nameaddress.Email;
      consignee.Account = nameaddress.Account;

      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = GetKeyValue('shipper', nameaddress.CustomData);
      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince.toUpperCase();
    }
  };

// Source: WILLIAMS-SONOMA (WSintl) (WSintl)_WSIntl Reference Rule_75.cs
// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        this.ValidateShipment(shipmentRequest);
        //var userId = userContext.UserId;
        var ConsigneeCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
        var ref1 = GetKeyValue('Custom1', ConsigneeCustomData);
        var ref2 = GetKeyValue('Custom2', ConsigneeCustomData);
        var ref3;
        var account = GetKeyValue('Custom3', ConsigneeCustomData);
        //Begin Determine Shipper
        if (account === "0000A0031E") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "OTHER_A0031E";
        }
        if (account === "0000A0027E") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "OTHER";
        }
        if (account === "0000872A2E") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "OTHER_872A2E";
        }
        if (account === "000033A17X") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "AUS";
        }
        if (account === "00007W7182") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "UK";
        }
        if (account === "00005R86R0") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "SG_5R86R0";
        }
        if (account === "00005R852X") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "SG_5R852X";
        }
        //End Determine Shipper
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = ref1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = ref2;
        //Begin Determine Service
        var Code = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Code;
        var SvcIdx = Code.lastIndexOf("-");
        if (SvcIdx === -1) {
            //var Service = { "Symbol": "UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS Adapter)" };
            var Service = { "Symbol": "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EPD", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS ConnectShip)" };
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = Service;
        } else {
            var ServiceCode = Code.substring(SvcIdx + 1, SvcIdx + 2);
            if (ServiceCode === "E") {
                //var ServiceE = { "Symbol": "UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS Adapter)" };
                var ServiceE = { "Symbol": "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EPD", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS ConnectShip)" };
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = ServiceE;
            }
            if (ServiceCode === "S") {
                //var ServiceS = { Symbol: "UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER", "Name": "UPS Saver (UPS Adapter)"  };
                var ServiceS = { "Symbol": "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPSVR", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS ConnectShip)" };
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = ServiceS;
            }
        }
        //End Determine Service
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = ref1;
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1) {
                ref3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1;
            } else {
                ref3 = "";
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ConsigneeReference = ref2 + " " + ref3;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference19 = userId;
        }
    };

// ValidateShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.ValidateShipment = function(shipmentRequest){
    if(shipmentRequest.Packages.length>20)
    { 
        throw {errorCode:999,message:"You cannot ship more than 20 packages."};
    }
    var weight = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight;
    var weightLimit = 0;
    var totalWeight = 0;
    if(weight.Units==="LB"){
            weightLimit = 150;
    }else{
        weightLimit = 68;
    }
    var i;
    for(i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++)
    {
        var pkgWeight = parseFloat(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount);
       totalWeight += pkgWeight;
    }
    if(totalWeight > weightLimit){
        throw {errorCode:999,message:"You cannot ship greater than " + weightLimit + " " + weight.Units + ".  Total Weight: "+ totalWeight + " " + weight.Units};
    }
}

// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
        
        if (this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration !== undefined){
                 this.GetWeight(); 
        }
        
        //alert(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Amount);
        userParams.cbrWeight = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Amount;

        
        loadValue = loadValue.trim();
        var validate = validateOrderValue(loadValue);
        if (validate === "EMPTY") {
            alert("LOAD VALUE REQUIRED PLEASE");
        }
        userParams.orderType = validate;   
        console.log(userParams);
       
    }; 

// this.GetWeight() // returns void
this.GetWeight = function () {
        if (this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration !== null) {
           
            var url = "https://localhost:5001/api/Scale/Read";
            var data ={
                "PortType": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.PortType,
                "Port": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.Port,
                "UsbVid": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.UsbVid,
                "UsbPid": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.UsbPid,
                "RequestCommand": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RequestCommand,
                "StopBits": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.StopBits,
                "Parity": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Parity,
                "RequestTimeout": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RequestTimeout,
                "HostAddress": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.HostAddress,
                "RegexPattern": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RegexPattern,
                "DeviceParser": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.DeviceParserType,
                "DeviceName": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Name,
                "Handshake": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Handshake
            };
            var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: data, async: false }).responseJSON;
            //debugger;
            console.log(data);
            console.log(ret);
            
            if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                
                this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].Weight = {
                    "Amount": ret.Weight,
                    "Units": "LB"
                };
               
                if (ret.HasDimensions) {
                    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].Dimensions = {
                        "Length": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[0],
                        "Width": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[1],
                        "Height": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[2],
                        //"Units": ret.DimensionUnit.toUpperCase() === "IN" ? 0 : 1
                        "Units": "In"
                    };
                }
            }
        }
    };

// function validateOrderValue(val) // returns string validation status
    function validateOrderValue(val) {
        if ((isEmpty(val)) === false) {
            var apicallpattern = /^(61|42|57)\d{8}(\-\d{1,2})?$/;   // Actual WOODLAND
            if (apicallpattern.test(val) === true) {
                return "VALIDAPI";
            }
            else { return "MANUAL"; }
            }   
            else { return "EMPTY"; }
    }

// function isEmpty(str) // returns boolean
    function isEmpty(str) {
        return (!str || 0 === str.length);
    }

// function sbrMessage(shipment) // returns boolean
    function sbrMessage(shipment) {
        return (shipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode === undefined || shipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode === 0)
        && (shipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== undefined && shipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== 'No error' && shipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null);
    }

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.buildShipment = this.BuildShipment;
        this.vm.getUserContext = this.GetUserContext;
        this.vm.postalCodeLookup = this.PostalCodeLookup;
        this.vm.thinClientAPIRequest = this.ThinClientAPIRequest;
        this.vm.createShipmentAutoSubmit = this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit;

        shipmentRequest.selectAddress = this.SelectAddress;
        shipmentRequest.updateNameAddressCSZ = this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = this.vm.profile.Shippers[0].Symbol;

        client.shipping.consigneeCompanyFocus();
    }

// function BuildShipment(ret) // returns void
    this.BuildShipment = function (ret) {
        client.shipping.buildShipmentModalHide();

        var weightPerPackage;
        var multiPackage = this.currentShipment.Packages.length > 1;

        if (ret.TotalWeight !== undefined && ret.TotalWeight !== 0 && ret.TotalWeight !== "")
            weightPerPackage = (ret.TotalWeight / ret.TotalPackages).toFixed(3);

        for (var i = 0; i < ret.TotalPackages; i++) {
            this.packageIndex = this.currentShipment.Packages.length - 1;
            if (i > 0 || multiPackage) {
                this.addPackage();
                multiPackage = true;
            }

            if (weightPerPackage !== undefined)
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Amount = weightPerPackage;
            if (ret.WeightUnit !== undefined)
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Units = ret.WeightUnit;
            else
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Units = this.translations.WeightUnit;
        }
        this.totalPackages = this.currentShipment.Packages.length;

        ret.TotalWeight = '';
        ret.TotalPackages = '';
    }

// function PostalCodeLookup(addressName) // returns void
    this.PostalCodeLookup = function (addressName) {
debugger;
        var userContext = this.getUserContext(this);
        var postalCode = $('[address-property-name="' + addressName + '"] [name="postalCode"]').val();
        var content = { AddressName: addressName, PostalCode: postalCode };
        var payload = { Action: 'CSZ', Content: JSON.stringify(content) };
        var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(payload), UserContext: userContext };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).responseJSON;
        if (response.ErrorCode > 0) {
            client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', response.ErrorMessage)
        } else {
            var responseData = JSON.parse(client.htmlText(response.Data));        
            if (responseData == null) {
                client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', 'Invalid or Not US Postal Code');
            } else {
                if (responseData.length > 1) {
                    this.addressResults = responseData;
                    client.shipping.validateAddressModalShow();
                } else {
                    this.currentShipment.updateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, responseData[0].City, responseData[0].StateProvince)
                }
            }
        }
    }

// function UpdateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, city, stateProvince) // returns void
    this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ = function (addressName, city, stateProvince) {
        var nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (addressName == 'ReturnAddress') {
            if (this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress == undefined)
                this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {};
            nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress;
        }
        nameAddress.City = city;
        nameAddress.StateProvince = stateProvince;
    }

// function SelectAddress(address) // returns void
    this.SelectAddress = function (address) {
        client.shipping.validateAddressModalHide();
        this.updateNameAddressCSZ(address.AddressName, address.City, address.StateProvince);
    }

// function CreateShipmentAutoSubmit(keyEvent) // returns void
    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {
        if (keyEvent.keyCode === 13 || keyEvent.keyCode === 9) {            
            event.preventDefault();
debugger;
            var $createShipmentBtn = $('#createShipmentBtn');
            var createShipmentInput = '#buildShipmentModalBody input';

            if (document.activeElement.id == $createShipmentBtn.attr('id')) {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // click on create build button if sending tab or enter while focus is on button
                    $createShipmentBtn.click();
                }
            } else {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // allow shipper chance to change weight unit
                    $createShipmentBtn.focus();
                }
            }
        }

        function isInputsEmpty($inputs) {
            var inputsIsEmpty = false;
            $inputs.each(function () {
                if (this.type == 'text') {
                    if (this.value.trim() == "") {
                        this.focus();
                        inputsIsEmpty = true;
                        return false;
                    };
                };
            });
            return inputsIsEmpty;
        }
    }

    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {

                }
            }
        }
